### [1] [The next-to-leading order of the differential cross-section of the subprocess of Compton scattering of quark-gluon of prompt photon production in proton-proton collisions at NICA energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19389)
*Mohsun Rasim Alizada,Azar Inshalla Ahmadov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文计算了在NICA能量下质子-质子碰撞中Compton散射子过程$qg \rightarrow qγ$的次领头阶微分截面，包括纵向极化和非极化两种情况。结果表明，次领头阶修正占领头阶的约15%，且极化对次领头阶的影响更为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在NICA能区精确预测直接光子产生过程的截面，需要超越领头阶近似，考虑次领头阶QCD修正，同时评估质子纵向极化对该过程的影响。

Method: 对Compton散射子过程$qg \rightarrow qγ$进行次领头阶（NLO）微扰QCD计算，分别考虑非极化和纵向极化两种情况，并与领头阶（LO）结果进行对比。

Result: 次领头阶修正贡献显著，约占领头阶结果的15%；质子纵向极化对次领头阶计算结果的影响大于对领头阶的影响。

Conclusion: 在高能质子-质子碰撞中，次领头阶QCD修正不可忽略，且极化效应在更高阶修正中更为突出，对精确理解NICA能区直接光子产生具有重要意义。

Abstract: In the presented article, the next-to-the-leading-order calculation of the differential cross-section of the Compton scattering subprocess $qg \rightarrow qγ$ for prompt photon production in proton-proton collisions at NICA energies has been carried out, both without and taking into account the longitudinal polarization of colliding protons.
  It is shown that the contribution of the next-to-leading order to the differential cross-section is significant at high energies of colliding protons and constitutes around $15\%$ of the leading-order calculation. The influence of the polarization of colliding protons on the next-to-leading-order calculation is more significant than on the leading-order calculation.

</details>


### [2] [Emergent Gauge Symmetries in Particle Physics and Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19403)
*Steven D. Bass*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了标准模型可能是一种涌现理论的观点，其规范对称性在紫外区域的某种相变中消失。希格斯真空的亚稳定性可能指向极高能标下的新临界现象。暗能量标度与轻马约拉纳中微子质量大小相近，两者都出现在涌现标度（约10^16 GeV）的低能展开同一阶。暗物质候选者包括轴子和涌现标度以上自由度的声子激发。可能的检验涉及中微子和原初引力波信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨规范对称性的起源，提出标准模型可能是涌现理论，而非基本理论，旨在解决规范对称性的来源这一基本问题，并解释希格斯真空亚稳定性、暗能量标度与中微子质量之间的关系。

Method: 基于涌现理论框架，从低能有效场论视角展开分析，利用逆涌现标度（约10^16 GeV）的低能展开，将暗能量和Majorana中微子质量作为同一阶的涌现现象处理。

Result: 暗能量标度与轻Majorana中微子质量在数量级上自然相近，均出现在10^16 GeV涌现标度的低能展开同一阶。轴子和涌现标度以上自由度的声子激发可作为暗物质候选。

Conclusion: 标准模型可能是一种涌现理论，其规范对称性在紫外相变中消失。中微子和原初引力波信号是检验该方案的重要实验途径。

Abstract: Where do gauge symmetries come from? These lectures develop the idea that the Standard Model might be emergent, with its gauge symmetries dissolving in some phase transition deep in the ultraviolet. The (meta-)stability of the Higgs vacuum may be pointing to some new critical phenomena at very high energy scales, with the Higgs connecting physics at LHC laboratory energies to that in the deep ultraviolet. In the emergence scenario, the dark energy scale comes out similar to the size of light Majorana neutrino masses. These two quantities appear at the same order in a low energy expansion in inverse powers of the scale of emergence, about $10^{16}$ GeV. Dark matter candidates include axions and phonon like excitations of degrees of freedom above the scale of emergence. Possible tests of these ideas involve neutrinos as well as gravitational-waves-related signals from the early Universe, which are sensitive to physics at very high energy scales.

</details>


### [3] [LeWRON: Agentic Analysis of Electroweak Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19425)
*Isaac R. Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: LeWRON是一个智能体框架，能够从输入拉格朗日量出发，全自动编排有限温度有效势构建、热历史追踪、气泡成核率计算和引力波谱预测的电弱相变分析流程，支持复现已有结果和探索新模型，并通过审计模块确保可复现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电弱相变分析涉及从构建有限温度有效势到计算气泡成核率、预测引力波谱等一系列技术上复杂、对约定敏感且依赖模型的分析流程，现有工具链分散、手动操作易出错且缺乏可复现性，因此需要自动化、可审计的框架来统一和简化这一过程。

Method: LeWRON采用智能体（agentic）架构，核心包括：审计工具箱构造模块用于生成模型特定代码；Explorer模块执行参数扫描和绘图等进一步分析；审计（auditor）智能体对中间分析输出进行检查；结构化构件（structured artifacts）存储中间结果以支持人工审查；支持复现模式（从文献推断约定并复现已发表结果）和发现模式（通过结构化检查点引导用户探索新模型）；提供命令行界面和Python API。

Result: 在多个代表性超出标准模型（BSM）场景上展示了LeWRON的有效性，并已公开发布代码在GitHub上。

Conclusion: LeWRON首次实现了电弱相变全分析流程的端到端自动化与可审计化，显著降低了该领域的技术门槛，提高了可复现性和科研效率，为连接粒子物理唯象学、重子生成和引力波观测提供了标准化工具。

Abstract: The electroweak phase transition (EWPT) is a central topic in particle physics and cosmology, connecting collider phenomenology, baryogenesis, and gravitational-wave observatories. Its analysis requires a technically demanding, convention-sensitive, and model-dependent pipeline, from constructing the finite-temperature effective potential to tracking thermal histories, computing bubble nucleation rates, and predicting gravitational-wave spectra. We present LeWRON (Learning ElectroWeak phase tRansitiON), an agentic framework that orchestrates this pipeline starting from an input Lagrangian. LeWRON combines audited toolbox construction with an Explorer module that uses the generated model-specific code for further analysis, including scans and plots. Intermediate analytic outputs are checked by auditor agents and stored as structured artifacts, enabling reproducible human inspection and downstream use through both a command-line interface and a public Python API. The framework supports a reproduction mode, which infers conventions from the literature and reproduces published results, and a discovery mode, which guides users through structured checkpoints for new models. We demonstrate LeWRON across representative beyond-the-Standard-Model scenarios and release the code on GitHub.

</details>


### [4] [Partial-wave unitarity and long-range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19432)
*Ryan Plestid,Pablo Quílez Lasanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究针对含无质量粒子理论中t道（前向散射）奇异性导致分波振幅在固定阶微扰论中定义不良的问题，提出了一种修正微扰论方法。通过纳入长程相互作用（特别是离壳Coulomb模），发现前向散射区域存在普适描述，使得振幅与重整化标度无关。所得分波振幅成为定义良好的单标度量，消除了对红外正则化器的虚假依赖，并给出了逐阶计算的实用方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 含无质量粒子的理论中，前向散射奇异性使得标准固定阶微扰论下的分波振幅发散，无法进行系统可改进的分波幺正性约束。现有方法依赖于红外正则化（如光子质量或维数正规化），导致虚假标度依赖，亟需构建一种内在自洽的、不依赖红外截断的分波展开框架。

Method: 本文采用修正微扰论，通过系统纳入离壳Coulomb模等长程相互作用，重新定义前向散射区域的边界行为。引入了普适的重新求和方案，将奇异性吸收进可重整化的量中，使得分波振幅在重整化标度下不变，并建立了逐阶微扰展开的实用计算流程。

Result: 建立了无质量粒子理论中分波振幅的普适单标度描述，证明该描述与重整化标度无关且不依赖于红外正则化方式。分波振幅成为定义良好的物理量，可在微扰论中逐阶可靠计算。

Conclusion: 本文为含无质量粒子的散射理论提供了系统可改进的分波幺正性分析方法，消除了长期存在的红外奇异性障碍，为量子电动力学、引力等理论中的非微扰界限研究奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Theories with massless particles contain $t$-channel (forward scattering) singularities that cause standard fixed order expressions for partial-wave amplitudes to be ill-defined. This presents an obstruction to systematically improvable partial-wave unitarity bounds. In this work, we study the construction of partial-wave amplitudes in a modified perturbation theory that incorporates long-range interactions focusing on the role of off-shell Coulomb modes. We find that there exists a universal description of the forward scattering region that renders the amplitudes renormalization scale independent. The resulting partial-wave amplitudes become well defined single-scale objects without spurious dependence on the infrared regulator, and we present a practical method for their computation order-by-order in perturbation theory.

</details>


### [5] [From Rags to Jeans: Axion Miniclusters from Early matter domination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19439)
*Ariel Angulo,Paola Arias,Nicolás Bernal,Javier Redondo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 早期物质主导时期，辐射浴的温度和密度不均匀性比标准辐射主导历史增长更高效。如果轴子质量依赖于温度，这些不均匀性会诱导轴子质量的空间波动，为轴子密度扰动提供新的源项。该机制在重加热温度刚好低于质量饱和尺度T_Λ时最有效，可使轴子过密度在物质-辐射相等时达到量级为1的量级。对于饱和暗物质丰度的QCD轴子，相等时的非线性谱呈现两个特征区域：一个与模驱动宇宙学中已存在的引力增强相关，另一个由轴子质量的温度依赖性产生。研究者估算了由此产生的迷你星团质量，并讨论了轴子迷你星团和轴子星亚结构的可能形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索早期物质主导时代中，温度依赖的轴子质量如何通过辐射浴不均匀性产生新的轴子密度扰动源，并研究这一机制对轴子暗物质结构和星团形成的潜在影响。

Method: 理论分析，研究早期物质主导时代中辐射浴不均匀性的增长，以及轴子质量温度依赖性诱导的空间波动作为轴子密度扰动的新源项。

Result: 该机制在重加热温度刚好低于T_Λ时最有效；QCD轴子饱和暗物质丰度时，相等时非线性谱呈现两个特征区域；估算了迷你星团质量。

Conclusion: 温度依赖的轴子质量在早期物质主导时代可作为轴子密度扰动的新源项，影响轴子迷你星团和轴子星的形成。

Abstract: In an early matter-dominated era, density and temperature inhomogeneities of the radiation bath grow more efficiently than in the standard radiation-dominated history. If the axion mass depends on temperature, these inhomogeneities induce spatial fluctuations of the axion mass, providing a new source term for axion density perturbations. We show that this mechanism is most efficient when the reheating temperature lies just below the mass-saturation scale $T_Λ$, and can drive axion overdensities to order unity by matter--radiation equality. For the QCD axion saturating the observed dark matter abundance, the nonlinear spectrum at equality exhibits two characteristic regions: one associated with the gravitational enhancement already present in moduli-driven cosmologies, and another produced by the temperature dependence of the axion mass. We estimate the resulting minicluster masses and discuss the possible formation of axion miniclusters and axion-star substructure.

</details>


### [6] [Spin Identification of Dark Sector Mediators through Angular Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19543)
*D. Aristizabal Sierra,S. Fuenzalida Garrido,F. Kling,T. Mäkelä,N. Viaux*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种仅基于衰变产物四动量即可重建的角度观测量，用于区分轻长寿命暗区粒子是标量还是矢量，并证明DUNE、SHiP和FASER2实验在大量未约束参数空间区域中能够识别出中介粒子的自旋。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在寻找轻长寿命暗区粒子的实验中，一旦发现此类粒子，下一步需要确定其量子数（自旋）。目前缺乏有效的方法仅从衰变产物的运动学信息区分标量和矢量粒子。

Method: 识别出一种角度观测量，该观测量仅通过衰变产物的四动量即可重建。对于来自轻介子衰变的矢量玻色子，该观测量呈现各向异性分布；对于标量粒子则呈现各向同性分布。

Result: 在DUNE、SHiP和FASER2实验的大规模未约束参数空间区域中，该角度观测量能够有效识别中介粒子的自旋。

Conclusion: 提出了一种仅依赖运动学信息区分标量与矢量暗区粒子的方法，并验证了未来实验的可行性。

Abstract: A variety of experiments are operating or planned to search for displaced decays of light long-lived dark sector particles. In case such a state is discovered, the next step is determining its quantum numbers. We identify an angular observable, reconstructible solely from the decay products' four-momenta, that exhibits an anisotropic distribution for vector bosons from light meson decays and an isotropic distribution for scalars. We demonstrate that searches at DUNE, SHiP and FASER2 will be able to identify the mediator spin in sizable regions of yet unconstrained parameter space.

</details>


### [7] [Real and Virtual Propagation in Neutrino Oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19548)
*Kenji Nishiwaki,Kin-ya Oda,Juntaro Wada*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了真空中味振荡的传播时间依赖性问题。通过鞍点法严格计算相关积分，推导出在短传播时间下仍有效的味改变振幅扩展表达式。研究表明，振荡仅在传播时间超过由外波包能量不确定性和传播粒子衰变宽度共同决定的阈值时发生；短于该阈值时，中间粒子表现为纯虚态，无法在宏观距离上传播。这一结果意味着Jacob-Sachs定理在短传播时间下的适用精度高于此前预期。该形式化方法适用于中微子及其他传播粒子，未来能量分辨率的提升可能使这一阈值变得可观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视真空中味振荡的传播时间依赖性，弥补现有Jacob-Sachs（或Grimus-Stockinger）定理在短传播时间极限下描述的不足，探索振荡行为发生的物理阈值。

Method: 采用波包量子场论框架，利用鞍点法（saddle-point method）显式计算相关积分，推导出适用于短传播时间条件的味改变振幅扩展表达式。

Result: 发现振荡存在一个传播时间阈值，该阈值由外波包能量不确定性和传播粒子衰变宽度共同决定。低于该阈值时，中间粒子表现为纯虚态（purely virtual state），无法在宏观距离上传播。Jacob-Sachs定理在短传播时间下的适用精度高于此前预期。

Conclusion: 该形式化方法不仅适用于中微子，也适用于其他传播粒子。尽管从虚传播到实传播的转变通常发生在微观尺度，直接实验检验具有挑战性，但未来能量分辨率的提升可能使这一阈值变得可观测。

Abstract: We revisit flavor oscillations in vacuum in terms of the propagation time of intermediate states. In the limit of a long propagation time (or distance), degenerate intermediate states exhibit oscillatory behavior, as described by the Jacob--Sachs (or Grimus--Stockinger) theorem within wave-packet quantum field theory. By explicitly evaluating the relevant integrals using the saddle-point method, we derive an extended expression for the flavor-changing amplitude that remains valid even for shorter propagation times. We show that oscillations occur only when the propagation time exceeds a threshold set by the energy uncertainty of the external wave packets and by the decay width of the propagating particle. For shorter propagation, the intermediate particle behaves as a purely virtual state, in the sense that it cannot propagate over a macroscopic distance. Although a direct experimental test of the transition from virtual to real propagation is challenging, since it typically occurs at microscopic scales, our result implies that the Jacob--Sachs theorem holds to higher accuracy than previously expected, even at short propagation times. Our formalism applies not only to neutrinos but also to other propagating particles, and future improvements in energy resolution may make this threshold observable.

</details>


### [8] [Freeze-in at all couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19564)
*Andreas Goudelis,Andre Lessa,Lucas Magno Dantas Ramos,Thomas Reggio*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了带电母体冻结暗物质模型，特别关注宇宙再加热温度低于或等于理论质量标度的情形，发现玻尔兹曼抑制的暗物质产生允许更强的耦合，同时追踪母体和暗物质的数密度演化对可靠预测至关重要，并更新了LHC和轻子味破缺衰变对参数空间的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究宇宙再加热温度较低时带电母体冻结暗物质模型的暗物质产生机制，探索在玻尔兹曼抑制下更强的耦合可能性及其现象学后果。

Method: 对带电母体冻结暗物质模型进行综合分析，考虑再加热温度与理论质量标度可比或更低的情形，追踪暗物质和母体的数密度演化动力学，并结合LHC搜索和轻子味破缺衰变进行现象学约束更新。

Result: 发现再加热温度较低时玻尔兹曼抑制允许暗物质与标准模型热浴之间存在更强的耦合；母体因快速衰变而无法达到热平衡这一意外行为被揭示；更新了LHC和轻子味破缺衰变对可行参数空间的互补性约束。

Conclusion: 在低再加热温度场景中，追踪暗物质和母体的数密度演化是获得可靠预言的关键，且LHC与轻子味破缺搜索在探测宇宙学可行的参数空间上具有互补性。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive analysis of a charged parent freeze-in dark matter model, focusing on scenarios where the Universe reheats to a temperature comparable to or lower than the mass scales of the theory. In such configurations, dark matter production is Boltzmann-suppressed, allowing for stronger couplings between dark matter and the Standard Model thermal bath while still reproducing the observed relic abundance. We emphasize the non-trivial interplay between the reheating temperature, the mediator and dark matter masses and the coupling strength. We show that tracking the number density evolution of both dark matter and the mediator is essential to obtain reliable predictions, including unexpected behaviors such as the mediator non-equilibration due to fast decays. Lastly, we explore the phenomenological implications of this scenario, updating constraints from LHC searches and lepton flavour-violating decays and highlighting the complementarity of these searches in probing the cosmologically viable parameter space.

</details>


### [9] [Sensitivity of the photon-induced processes to the proton radius](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19604)
*Nikhil Krishna,Mariola Klusek-Gawenda,Rafal Staszewski*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过质子-质子碰撞中双轻子的独占产生过程来探测质子半径。使用偶极形状因子模型，比较了传统Λ²=0.71 GeV²与对应不同质子半径的PDG测试场景。对当前ATLAS和CMS数据的拟合得到Λ²=0.465±0.056 GeV²，对应有效半径rp=1.002±0.038 fm，表明对质子半径尺度具有非平凡的敏感性，但尚不能作为质子半径之谜的确定性解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用质子-质子碰撞中独占产生的双轻子过程作为探针，测量质子电荷半径，试图解决"质子半径之谜"（即不同实验方法测量的质子半径存在显著差异的问题）。

Method: 采用偶极形状因子模型，比较传统参数Λ²=0.71 GeV²与PDG测试场景中两种质子半径值（rp=0.8751 fm和rp=0.84087 fm）的差异。通过对ATLAS和CMS实验数据的拟合，提取形状因子参数Λ²并反推有效质子半径。

Result: 灵敏度在大双轻子不变质量和前向/后向快度区域最大。拟合ATLAS和CMS数据得到Λ²=0.465±0.056 GeV²，对应有效半径rp=1.002±0.038 fm，与传统的Λ²=0.71 GeV²（对应rp≈0.84 fm）存在显著偏离。

Conclusion: 独占双轻子产生过程对质子半径尺度具有非平凡的敏感性，但当前结果尚不能作为质子半径之谜的确定性解决方案，需要进一步的实验和理论研究。

Abstract: We study the exclusive production of dileptons in proton--proton collisions as a probe of the proton radius. Using a dipole form factor model, we compare the conventional choice of $Λ^2=0.71$~GeV$^2$ with PDG test scenarios corresponding to $r_p=0.8751$~fm and $r_p=0.84087$~fm. The sensitivity is greatest at large dilepton invariant masses and forward/backward rapidity. Fitting to the current ATLAS and CMS data within the adopted model gives $Λ^2 = 0.465 \pm 0.056~\mathrm{GeV}^2$, corresponding to an effective radius $r_p = 1.002 \pm 0.038~\mathrm{fm}$, which indicates non-trivial sensitivity on the proton radius scale, but is not yet a definitive solution to the proton radius puzzle.

</details>


### [10] [$U(1)_{B-L}$ Dark Matter Constrains Smooth (SUSY) Hybrid Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19612)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于超引力中的光滑混合暴胀机制，采用非最小Kähler势以控制超重力高阶修正；通过三个标量场（暴胀子$\sigma$、辅助场$\zeta$、中介子$\eta$）构建模型；暗物质作为受$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性保护的惰性标量，通过再热过程非热产生；通过观测暗物质遗迹丰度约束暴胀扇区参数空间。

Result: 再现观测暗物质遗迹丰度对暴胀扇区施加强约束，显著缩小允许参数空间；标量谱指数被严格限制为$n_s \simeq 0.972 - 0.974$，与当前观测一致；暴胀-暗物质耦合虽不影响背景演化，但会可观测地修改张标比和原初引力波谱。

Conclusion: 成功建立了暴胀动力学与暗物质产生之间的统一框架，暗物质物理可对暴胀可观测量（标量谱指数、张标比、原初引力波谱）产生可观测的影响，为通过宇宙学观测检验暗物质模型提供了新途径。

Abstract: We propose a unified framework that connects inflationary dynamics with dark matter production within a supersymmetric $U(1)_{B-L}$ extension of the Standard Model. The setup is based on smooth hybrid inflation embedded in supergravity, with a non-minimal Kahler potential ensuring control of higher-order corrections. The model involves three scalar fields: the inflaton $σ$, an auxiliary field $ζ$ responsible for ending inflation, and a singlet mediator $η$ that links the inflationary and dark sectors. Dark matter is realized as an inert scalar stabilized by a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry and produced non-thermally via reheating dynamics. We show that reproducing the observed dark matter relic abundance imposes strong constraints on the inflationary sector, significantly reducing the allowed parameter space. As a result, the scalar spectral index is tightly constrained to $n_s \simeq 0.972 - 0.974$, consistent with current observational bounds. While the inflaton-dark matter coupling has a negligible effect on the background evolution, it induces observable modifications in the tensor-to-scalar ratio and the spectrum of primordial gravitational waves. This establishes a direct link between dark matter physics and inflationary observables.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用IceCube宇宙射线缪子数据集，提出探测器内缪子到陶子（μ→τ）转换的新搜索方案；采用模型无关的有效场论（EFT）算符描述CLFV相互作用，并考虑轴矢量Z'模型作为EFT的具体实现；计算IceCube及下一代望远镜（IceCube-Gen2, HUNT）的灵敏度。

Abstract: Any observation of charged lepton flavor violation (CLFV) would be a clear signal of beyond-the-Standard-Model physics. Here, we propose a novel CLFV search using neutrino telescopes with their large cosmic-ray muon samples. Specifically, we use a recent IceCube cosmic-ray muon dataset and propose a new search for muon-to-tau conversion inside the IceCube detector. We illustrate our idea with CLFV interactions described by model-independent Effective Field Theory (EFT) operators and present the IceCube sensitivity on the relevant EFT scale. We also consider a specific realization of the EFT operator in terms of an axial-vector $Z'$ interaction and show sensitivities in the $Z'$ mass-coupling plane. We compare our sensitivities with those from low-energy CLFV searches, as well as from current and future collider experiments. We also show projections from next-generation neutrino telescopes, such as IceCube-Gen2 and HUNT, and demonstrate how neutrino telescopes can provide a powerful complementary probe of CLFV.

### [12] [Constraining ADD black holes at the LHC with $\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19839)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在ADD模型框架下，利用LHC在质心能量14 TeV、积分亮度349.4 fb⁻¹的数据，研究微观黑洞形成过程中的能量损失效应（参数ζ），给出了不同额外维数（D=3,7）和约化普朗克尺度（Λ_D=1,9 TeV）下黑洞质量M_B的排除上限，发现能量损失会显著降低质量极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于ADD模型，在√s=14 TeV、积分亮度349.4 fb⁻¹条件下，通过引入参数ζ（0≤ζ≤0.35）描述黑洞形成过程中的能量损失，计算不同额外维数D（3和7）及约化普朗克尺度Λ_D（1 TeV和9 TeV）下黑洞质量M_B的排除上限，并与无损失情形（ζ=0）对比。

Conclusion: 能量损失效应显著降低LHC对微观黑洞质量的排除能力，在制定实验搜索策略时必须考虑该因素；额外的空间维度数增加会略微提高排除极限，但能量损失的影响更为主导。

Abstract: We explore microscopic black holes at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) in the context of the ADD model for the centre-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s} = 14~\mathrm{TeV}$ at an integrated luminosity of $349.4~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and provide constraints on the black hole mass, $M_{\mathrm{B}}$ by taking into account the effects of loss during the formation process of black holes through the parameter $ζ$. Our analysis reveals that for $ζ= 0$, black holes with $M_{\mathrm{B}} \leq 11.83~\mathrm{TeV}$ are disfavored in the case of three extra dimensions ($\mathcal{D}$), for the reduced Planck scale ($Λ_{\mathcal{D}}$) of about a TeV. The corresponding values for $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 9~\mathrm{TeV}$ turned out to be about $10.33~\mathrm{TeV}$. A significant reduction in the aforementioned limits is observed while the loss gets higher, e.g. for $ζ= 0.35$, $M_{\mathrm{B}}$ reduces to $7.65 (6.82)~\mathrm{TeV}$ at $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 1 (9)~\mathrm{TeV}$. These limits change to $12.03 ~(10.88)~\mathrm{TeV}$ and $7.80~ (7.03)~\mathrm{TeV}$ respectively for $ζ= 0~(0.35)$ for $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 1 (9)~\mathrm{TeV}$ at 95\% C.L. in case $\mathcal{D}$ is raised to seven.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论预测与PDG实验值之间在J/ψ→γη_c辐射衰变的部分宽度和分支比上存在张力，现有实验提取方法使用经验阻尼函数修正光子能谱，导致可观测量存在固有歧义。

Abstract: We assess the tension between theoretical predictions and the values quoted by the Particle Data Group (PDG) for the partial decay width and branching fraction associated with the radiative charmonium decay $J/ψ\toγη_c$. A profile scan over the most recent PDG data depending on the branching fraction $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ suggests that the correlation between measured branching fractions is compatible with lattice QCD determinations of the partial decay widths $Γ(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ and $Γ(η_c\toγγ)$. We propose a theoretically grounded photon line shape for the radiative decay spectrum and a prescription for the extraction of (product) branching fractions involving the magnetic dipole (M1) transition $J/ψ\toγη_c$. This approach obviates the need to modify the photon energy spectrum line shape using empirical damping functions, as done in the most recent experimental extractions of $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ from the photon line shape, thereby eliminating an inherent ambiguity in the determination of the derived observables.

### [14] [New Avenues of Heavy Neutral Lepton at Muon Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19906)
*Fa-Xin Yang,Feng-Lan Shao,Zhi-Long Han,Honglei Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在多TeV缪子对撞机上，通过新矢量玻色子融合过程（$Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ 和 $Z'Z'\to NN$）产生重中性轻子$N$的机制，并分析了相应的轻子数破坏信号。不同于标准模型中的矢量玻色子融合过程，新过程不受小混合角$\alpha$压制，且即使在重希格斯$m_H>\sqrt{s}$时仍可行，为重中性轻子本征性质探测提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文考虑两种新矢量玻色子融合过程：含重希格斯的过程$Z'Z'\to H\to NN$和不含重希格斯的过程$Z'Z'\to NN$。在$U(1)$规范扩展的seesaw模型框架下，计算了这些过程的截面，并与标准模型矢量玻色子融合过程进行对比。随后对缪子对撞机上的轻子数破坏信号进行详细分析，研究末态包含$μ^+μ^-$和两个来自$N\to μ^\pm jj$衰变的信号，其中$W$玻色子衰变产生的两个喷注被合并为一个fat-jet $J$。

Result: 新过程$Z'Z'\to H\to NN$由于不依赖希格斯玻色子间的混合角$\alpha$，因此不受该参数压制，相比标准矢量玻色子融合过程具有显著优势。而$Z'Z'\to NN$过程在重希格斯质量$m_H>\sqrt{s}$时仍然可行，扩展了可探测的参数空间。通过详细分析轻子数破坏信号$μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- NN$（含/不含重希格斯）及$N\to μ^\pm jj$衰变，验证了这些新途径在探测重中性轻子方面的可行性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的新矢量玻色子融合过程为重中性轻子在多TeV缪子对撞机上的产生提供了替代且有效的探测途径。这些过程克服了标准矢量玻色子融合过程受小混合角压制的局限，并在更广泛的参数空间（包括重希格斯质量大于对撞能量的情况）中保持可行性，有助于揭示重中性轻子的本征特征。

Abstract: With initial state radiation, the multi-TeV muon collider can be regarded as an electroweak boson collider. The dominant production mode of the certain process becomes the vector boson fusion channel, because the corresponding cross section typically increases logarithmically at high energies. This also holds true for new physics beyond the standard model. Within the $U(1)$ gauged extension of seesaw models, the heavy neutral lepton has additional interactions with the new gauge boson $Z'$ and heavy Higgs $H$. In this paper, we investigate the production of heavy neutral lepton $N$ via the new vector boson fusion processes $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ with and $Z'Z'\to NN$ without heavy Higgs at the multi-TeV muon collider. Different from the canonical vector boson fusion processes $WW/ZZ\to H\to NN$, the new process $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ is not suppressed by the small mixing angle $α$ between the Higgs bosons. Meanwhile, the pair production process $Z'Z'\to NN$ is also viable even for heavy Higgs $m_H> \sqrt{s}$. Therefore, these new avenues provide alternative pathways to probe the intrinsic feature of the heavy neutral lepton. We then perform a detailed analysis of the lepton number violation signals via the new vector boson fusion with heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- H \to μ^+μ^- NN$ and without heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- NN$, followed by $N\to μ^\pm jj$, where the two jets from $W$ boson decay are treated as one fat-jet $J$.

Our two- and three-body analyses show sensitivity to effective baryon-level couplings of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6}-10^{-7})$ for MeV-scale recoil momenta. We establish a practical no-go result for a universal light charged scalar $φ^+$: with a first-generation $φ^+\bar u d$ coupling, existing electroweak-precision and beta-decay constraints are parametrically stronger than the projected LHCb sensitivity. We then identify a two-charm-selective charged-current portal whose leading operator has a nonzero matrix element in doubly charmed baryons but vanishes at leading order in pions, nucleons, nuclei, and singly charmed mesons. In this class of models, $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ transitions can provide the leading direct probe of the portal interaction.

*Miguel Crispim Romão,Stephen F. King*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次利用人工智能技术（NSGA-III）对双 flavo Froggatt-Nielsen 模型进行了系统性扫描。通过引入两个独立耦合至上、下扇区的 flavo 场，利用其真空期望值之间的相对相位作为 CP 破坏的自然来源，解决了单 flavo 模型无法解释 CP 破坏的问题。将寻找现象学可行模型构建为多目标优化问题，同时拟合 18 个 FN 电荷、45 个 Wilson 系数和 flavo 参数，发现超过 10 万个独特可行模型，支持中微子质量的正序和反序，并展示了最小 flavo 指数仅为 3 的模型以及无需连续参数优化即可达到 6% 精度的费米子质量拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准单 flavo Froggatt-Nielsen 模型无法提供 CP 破坏的自然来源，且其参数空间有限，难以同时解释夸克和轻子扇区的所有实验观测数据。本文旨在通过引入双 flavo 框架并利用 AI 技术探索高维、混合离散-连续参数空间，以寻找更丰富的现象学可行模型。

Method: 采用双 flavo Froggatt-Nielsen 框架，其中两个独立的 flavo 场分别耦合至上型和下型夸克扇区。将实验约束形式化为多目标优化问题，使用非支配排序遗传算法 III（NSGA-III）同时拟合 18 个 FN 电荷、45 个 Wilson 系数及 flavo 参数，覆盖夸克和轻子扇区。无需单独训练阶段，直接搜索现象学可行的模型。

Result: 发现超过 10 万个独特现象学可行模型，重复率极低，表明双 flavo FN 模型空间尚未被穷尽。中微子质量的正序和反序均能被实现。flavo 真空期望值的相对层级对无中微子双贝塔衰变有效质量 m_ee 产生定性不同的预言。发现了最小 flavo 指数仅为 3 的模型，以及无需连续参数优化即可将带电费米子质量拟合到 6% 精度的模型。

Conclusion: 双 flavo FN 框架为理解夸克和轻子扇区的质量层级与混合模式提供了丰富且尚未被穷举的理论空间。AI 驱动的多目标优化方法比先前的强化学习方法快数个数量级，为探索高维物理模型空间提供了高效的新范式。该框架自然包含了 CP 破坏来源，并对无中微子双贝塔衰变实验具有可检验的预言。

Abstract: We present the first systematic and comprehensive scan of two-flavon Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) models, employing artificial intelligence techniques to explore the high-dimensional, mixed discrete-continuous parameter space. Extending the standard single-flavon FN framework to a two-flavon setup in which separate flavon fields couple independently to the up- and down-type sectors, we demonstrate that the relative phase between their vacuum expectation values (vevs) provides a natural and generic source of CP violation absent in single-flavon models. To explore this enlarged model space, we cast the search for phenomenologically viable models as a multi-objective optimisation problem, formulating each experimental constraint as a separate objective, and employ the Non-dominated Sorting Genetic Algorithm III to simultaneously fit all 18 FN charges, 45 Wilson coefficients, and flavon parameters to both the quark and lepton sectors. Our approach requires no separate training phase and identifies phenomenologically viable models orders of magnitude faster than prior reinforcement learning methods. Imposing experimental constraints on CKM and PMNS mixing angles and CP phases, charged fermion masses, and neutrino squared-mass differences, we discover over $100\,000$ unique viable models with a remarkably low duplication rate, indicating that the space of valid two-flavon FN realisations has not been exhausted. Both Normal and Inverted neutrino mass squared orderings are realised, with the relative hierarchy between the flavon vevs producing qualitatively distinct predictions for the effective neutrinoless double beta decay mass $m_{ee}$. We further demonstrate the existence of minimal FN realisations with maximal flavon exponent as small as three, and of models reproducing charged fermion masses to within $6\%$ without any dedicated continuous parameter optimisation.

</details>


### [18] [Non-standard decays of vector-like top partners in a $2$-Higgs doublet model at the HL-LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20054)
*Tanumoy Mandal,Stefano Moretti,Rachit Sharma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在高亮度大型强子对撞机（HL-LHC）上，通过矢量-like顶夸克（T）衰变到带电希格斯粒子（H±），随后H±→τν，产生包含两个τ轻子、两个b喷注和缺失横动量的末态，来探测非标准VLQ衰变的前景。模型无关分析利用全局运动学观测量压制本底，并利用τ极化敏感观测量作为互补探针。结果显示，在3 ab⁻¹积分亮度下，该通道对VLQ质量可达约1.9 TeV的发现级灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在包含扩展标量区和矢量-like费米子的理论框架中，矢量-like夸克（VLQ）可能具有涉及额外希格斯粒子的非标准衰变模式，这些模式在现有实验搜索中尚未被充分探索。因此，需要研究如何利用HL-LHC探测这类新物理信号。

Method: 针对T→H±b、H±→τν的级联衰变链，进行模型无关的唯象学分析。利用全局运动学观测量（基于可见粒子和缺失横动量矢量）压制主要本底，同时构建基于强子衰变τ极化敏感观测量作为互补探针，使用Asimov显著性评估发现灵敏度。

Result: 2τ + 2b + 缺失横动量通道为搜索非标准VLQ衰变提供了有前景且与现有搜索正交的途径，在3 ab⁻¹积分亮度和√s=14 TeV条件下，对VLQ质量可达约1.9 TeV的发现级灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该通道有望在HL-LHC上实现对扩展希格斯扇区中非标准VLQ衰变的发现级探测，VLQ质量上限约为1.9 TeV，为未来实验搜索提供了新的方向。

Abstract: Extensions of the Standard Model featuring both an enlarged scalar sector and vector-like fermions arise naturally in a wide class of well-motivated theoretical frameworks. In such scenarios, vector-like Quarks (VLQs) can exhibit non-standard decay modes involving additional Higgs states, giving rise to distinctive collider signatures that remain largely unexplored by existing experimental searches. We investigate the prospects of probing this possibility at the high-luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC) through the decay of vector-like top partner ($T$) to charged Higgs ($H^{\pm}$) followed by the decay, $H^\pm\toτν$, producing a final state containing two tau leptons, two $b$-jets, and missing transverse energy. A model-independent collider analysis is performed using global kinematic observables constructed from visible objects and the missing transverse momentum vector to suppress the dominant backgrounds. Polarization-sensitive observables built from the hadronic $τ$ decay products are also examined as complementary probes of the spin-$0$ origin of the $τ$ leptons. The expected discovery sensitivity is evaluated using the Asimov significance for an integrated luminosity of $3$ ab$^{-1}$ at $\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV. Our results demonstrate that the $2τ\:+\:2b\:+$ missing $E_T$ channel provides a promising and largely orthogonal avenue to search for non-standard VLQ decays in extended Higgs sectors, with discovery-level sensitivity achievable for VLQ masses up to approximately $1.9$ TeV.

A replica-based strategy consistently quantifies perturbative missing-higher-order effects (F-MHOUs) and nonperturbative wave-function uncertainties (F-NPWFs), yielding the first uncertainty-resolved fragmentation-function set for the $Ω_{3Q}$ sector. The resulting LHAPDF6 grids are employed to investigate semi-inclusive $Ω_{3Q}$ plus jet production at the HL-LHC and future FCC within the (sym)JETHAD environment. Method: 采用半解析计算反弹作用并与CosmoTransitions数值结果对比；利用包含哈勃膨胀和温度演化的三维Langevin晶格模拟研究相变实时演化；基于相变参数估算气泡碰撞和等离子体声学运动产生的引力波谱。

Abstract: We investigate the first-order phase transition that terminates thermal inflation and evaluate the associated stochastic gravitational-wave signals. The transition is first characterized through semi-analytic calculations of the bounce action, which are compared with numerical results obtained using CosmoTransitions. We then study its real-time evolution in a three-dimensional Langevin lattice simulation that incorporates Hubble expansion and the corresponding temperature evolution throughout the transition. The lattice dynamics are consistent with the bounce-action estimates: the transition proceeds through localized bubble nucleation and subsequent bubble growth, rather than through a phase-mixing instability. Using the resulting transition parameters, we estimate the gravitational-wave spectra generated by bubble collisions and acoustic motions in the plasma. The predicted stochastic background lies within the projected sensitivity ranges of future gravitational-wave observatories, including BBO and DECIGO.

### [21] [The Simplest Dirac Scoto-Seesaw Realization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20119)

Method: 采用反常自由的U(1)_{B-L}规范对称性，对右手中微子赋予手征性电荷(-4,-4,5)，通过树图生成大气中微子质量平方差，辐射修正产生太阳中微子质量平方差；自发对称破缺后残留Z_6对称性稳定暗物质；研究了两种最小实现方案。

Abstract: We present a simple Dirac scoto-seesaw framework based on the anomaly-free $U(1)_{B-L}$ charge assignment $(-4,-4,5)$ for $ν_R$. This chiral charge assignment naturally accounts for the observed neutrino mass-squared differences, with $Δm^2_{\rm atm}$ generated at tree level and $Δm^2_{\rm sol}$ arising radiatively. After the spontaneous breaking of gauged $U(1)_{B-L}$, a residual $Z_6$ symmetry stabilizes the dark matter candidate. We investigate two minimal realizations of the framework, finding that both normal and inverted orderings are viable in one case, whereas only normal ordering survives in the other, with distinctive features for neutrino observables. Moreover, the chiral nature of the $U(1)_{B-L}$ charges suppresses the dilepton branching fraction of $Z'$, resulting in weaker ATLAS mass bounds than in the conventional vector $B-L$ scenario, thereby easing constraints on the dark sector. We explore the dark matter phenomenology of the singlet scalar and fermionic dark matter candidates. While singlet scalar DM is often severely constrained, the presence of the $Z'$ portal together with annihilation and co-annihilation channels substantially broadens the allowed parameter space. Thus, the framework offers a predictive scenario for neutrino and dark matter phenomenology that can be probed in future experiments.

### [23] [String Axiverse Enhancement of Superradiant Dark Matter Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20524)
*Diogo S. Gorgulho,Jacob A. Litterer,João G. Rosa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了弦论中大量轻轴子（~100-10^5种）对原初黑洞产生的暗物质的影响。通过霍金辐射和超辐射两种机制，发现大量轴子种类会增强超辐射效率并扩大微玻色子星作为暗物质候选者的参数空间，但轴子种类过多会导致黑洞蒸发过快而限制超辐射云的最大质量。此外，蒸发产生的轴子对复合时代的相对论自由度贡献可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多考虑单一或少数轴子物种，但弦论构型自然预言大量轻轴子（轴子景观），需要研究这一特性如何影响原初黑洞的暗物质产生机制，特别是超辐射和霍金辐射的相互作用。

Method: 理论分析：结合弦论轴子景观（~100-10^5种轻轴子）、原初黑洞的霍金蒸发与超辐射机制、以及暗物质形成的微玻色子星模型，系统分析轴子种类数对黑洞自旋演化、超辐射云增长、以及暗物质丰度的参数空间约束。

Result: (1) 大量轴子种类通过增加黑洞自旋显著提升超辐射效率；(2) 扩大了微玻色子星作为暗物质的可行参数区间（暗物质质量、黑洞质量与自旋）；(3) 轴子种类过多会导致PBH蒸发过快，限制超辐射云达到最大质量；(4) PBH蒸发产生的轴子对复合时代有效中微子种类数的贡献极小，不可观测。

Conclusion: 弦轴子景观显著改变原初黑洞通过超辐射产生暗物质的图景，既扩展了微玻色子星作为暗物质的参数空间（有利），又存在因蒸发过快导致的上限约束（制约）。蒸发轴子对宇宙学观测（如Neff）无影响。

Abstract: We study the effects of string axion emission on dark matter production by light primordial black holes (PBHs), through both evaporation and superradiance. We show, in particular, that the Hawking emission of $\mathcal{O}(100-10^5)$ light axion species predicted in realistic string theory constructions can significantly enhance the efficiency of superradiance, given the associated increase in the PBH spin. The string axiverse thus significantly expands the parametric regions (dark matter mass and PBH mass and spin) for which a sizeable fraction of dark matter may presently be in the form of ``micro-boson stars'': the self-gravitating remnants of superradiant dark matter clouds. Conversely, for too large a number of axion species PBHs evaporate too quickly for superradiant clouds to attain their maximum mass. Finally, assuming that all dark matter is produced by PBHs (through both superradiance and Hawking emission), we show that the axions emitted during PBH evaporation give an immeasurably small contribution to the relativistic degrees of freedom at recombination.

### [24] [Three-particle di-light-cone distribution amplitudes of the $B$-meson in heavy-quark effective theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20267)
*Riccardo Bartocci,Philipp Böer,Thorsten Feldmann,Max Ferré,Nico Gubernari,Daniel Vladimirov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对B介子的三粒子双光锥分布振幅(DLCDAs)进行了系统性研究，定义了八种独立分布振幅并建立了扭度分类，利用局域算符恒等式和运动方程约束推导了归一化积分和一阶矩的树级关系，构建了动量空间模型，并对领先扭度分布引入了α_s阶辐射修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有和非轻子B介子衰变中存在不可因子化的软胶子贡献，需要新的非微扰参量来描述这些动力学过程，而传统的B介子光锥分布振幅无法完全刻画软场与两个不同方向准直自由度耦合的构型。

Method: 通过定义B介子到真空的三定域HQET算符矩阵元（轻反夸克和胶子场强张量位于两条背靠背光线上），完成完整的洛伦兹分解，识别出八个独立DLCDAs并按扭度分类；利用局域算符恒等式和运动方程约束得到树级关系；对领先扭度分布引入α_s阶微扰辐射尾。

Result: 建立了包含八个独立分布振幅的完整体系，获得了归一化积分和一阶矩关于最小化强子参数集的树级关系，构建了动量空间模型，并给出了领先扭度分布包含α_s辐射修正的参数化形式。

Conclusion: 该研究为不可因子化软胶子贡献提供了系统的非微扰描述框架，有助于提升稀有和非轻子B介子衰变的理论预言精度。

Abstract: We present a systematic study of the three-particle di-light-cone distribution amplitudes (DLCDAs) of the $B$-meson. They are defined through $B$-meson--to--vacuum matrix elements of trilocal HQET operators, in which the light antiquark and the gluon field-strength tensor are located on two back-to-back light rays. In this sense, the DLCDAs generalise the conventional $B$-meson light-cone distribution amplitudes to configurations where soft fields couple to collinear degrees of freedom in two distinct directions. As such, they parametrise the non-perturbative dynamics associated with non-factorisable soft-gluon contributions in rare and non-leptonic exclusive $B$-meson decays. We derive the complete Lorentz decomposition of the matrix elements of generic trilocal operators, identify eight independent DLCDAs, and organise them in a basis of definite twist. Using local operator identities and equations-of-motion constraints, we obtain tree-level relations for their normalisation integrals and first moments in terms of a minimal set of hadronic parameters. These relations allow us to construct simple momentum-space models for all independent DLCDAs. For the leading-twist distribution, we further incorporate the perturbative radiative tail at order $α_s$ and discuss its impact on the resulting parametrisation.

</details>


### [25] [Dyonic lattices, $θ$-angles and axions in the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20319)

Abstract: We investigate the implications of the Witten effect in the Standard Model with a general global gauge group structure and determine the values of the three $θ$-parameters that lead to distinct families of allowed spectra of dyons. We construct and classify the corresponding dyonic charge lattices consistent with the Standard Model gauge structure. This approach enables us to re-derive the known global-group--dependent periodicities of the $θ$ angles and to determine all CP-invariant points in $θ$-space. The electromagnetic subgroup $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ is shown to arise \emph{prior} to electroweak symmetry breaking by factoring out the effect of the anomalous $B+L$ transformations, which reduces the physical $θ$-parameter space from a three-torus to a two-torus. Our phenomenological conclusions include an observation that a discovery of a $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ monopole carrying non-zero electric charge would determine the last remaining unknown parameter of the Standard Model. Lastly we study how $θ$-space shapes axion physics with emphasis on the axion-photon coupling and show that a single axion is insufficient to render the Standard Model vacuum fully CP invariant.

Conclusion: 对于LDMX和DarkSHINE实验，现有的相干Bethe-Heitler框架足以描述暗光子信号；而LOHENGRIN实验则需要在探测器设计上增加HCAL扩展以应对衍射散射本底。

So far, the signal characteristics, i.e. the behavior of the recoiling electron, have mostly been studied in coherent Bethe-Heitler electron-nucleus scattering with a dark photon that couples only to the Standard Model charged leptons. In this work, we present the calculations of the differential cross sections of all contributing real emission processes up to third order in the electromagnetic fine structure constant and fourth order in the kinetic mixing parameter associated with the dark photon. We consider a dark photon coupling to both the beam electron and the hadronic target and we take into account the scattering off both the target nucleus and its nuclear constituents. Besides real emission processes, we also discuss virtual dark photon contributions and their relevance for the signal prediction. After discussing the different phase space regions and constraints emerging from the experimental setups, we show numerical results of the cross sections and differential distributions, including the signal and dominant background. Within our framework, we find that the LOHENGRIN experiment will require an extension of its HCAL to effectively veto background processes originating from diffractive scattering. Apart from that, the contributions beyond coherent Bethe-Heitler scattering, in the presence of realistic experimental selections, have only a limited effect on the predicted signal and background in the relevant dark photon mass range.

### [29] [New Gauge Forces, Neutron Stars and Schwinger Neutrino Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20393)
*Yuxin Liu,Zhen Liu,Andrey Shkerin,Jing Shu,Yue Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由$B-L$、$L_e-L_{μ/τ}$或$L_μ-L_τ$规范对称性产生的新长程力对中微子的影响。天体（如地球、太阳或中子星）产生的轻子势会导致带电中微子的Schwinger对产生。反号电荷粒子在势阱中积累形成简并费米气体，同号电荷粒子则形成稳定中微子通量逃逸。对于$B-L$和$L_e-L_{μ/τ}$力，效应太弱无法观测；对于$L_μ-L_τ$力，当中微子耦合常数$g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$时在中子星中效应显著。该μ子力改变了中子星在平衡状态下的元素丰度并抑制了其$L_μ-L_τ$电荷，从而使得从中子星并合得出的$g\gtrsim 10^{-17}$约束失效。此外，对于该量级的$g$，Schwinger效应产生的中微子通量可能从距离约100 pc的单个年轻中子星被探测到，典型中微子能量$E_ν\sim 100$ MeV。专门搜寻此类信号将重新确立$g\lesssim 10^{-18}$的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由新对称性（$B-L$、$L_e-L_{μ/τ}$或$L_μ-L_τ$）规范产生的新长程力在中微子物理中的可观测效应，特别关注中子星等致密天体环境中的中微子产生机制及其对现有天体物理约束的影响。

Method: 通过理论分析天体产生的轻子势导致的中微子Schwinger对产生机制，研究带电中微子在势阱中的积累与逃逸行为，并评估不同规范对称性下该效应的强度及其对中子星性质的影响。

Result: $B-L$和$L_e-L_{μ/τ}$力效应太弱不可观测；$L_μ-L_τ$力在$g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$时在中子星中效应显著，改变了元素丰度并抑制了电荷，使中子星并合约束失效。在$g\gtrsim 10^{-17}$时，Schwinger效应产生的中微子通量可能从距离约100 pc的单个年轻中子星被探测到。

Conclusion: 现有中子星并合对$L_μ-L_τ$力的约束被证明无效；专门搜索来自年轻中子星的Schwinger效应中微子信号将重新确立$g\lesssim 10^{-18}$的约束上限。

Abstract: We investigate neutrino effects of new long-range forces arising from gauging $B-L$, $L_e-L_{μ/τ}$ or $L_μ-L_τ$ symmetries of the Standard Model. The leptonic potential generated by astronomical bodies, such as the Earth, the Sun or a neutron star, results in the Schwinger pair production of neutrinos charged under the new gauge symmetry. The oppositely charged particles accumulate in the potential well forming a degenerate Fermi gas, while equally charged particles fly away forming a steady flux of neutrinos. We find that, for the $B-L$ and $L_e-L_{μ/τ}$ forces, these effects are too weak to be observable. For the $L_μ-L_τ$ force these effects are significant in neutron stars if the gauge coupling is $g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$. The muonic force changes the element abundances of a neutron star in equilibrium and suppresses its $L_μ-L_τ$ charge. This invalidates the constraint on $g$ from neutron star mergers, at $g\gtrsim 10^{-17}$. Furthermore, for such values of $g$, the neutrino flux produced by the Schwinger effect could potentially be detected from a single young neutron star at a distance of $\simeq 100$ pc, with the typical neutrino energy $E_ν\sim 100$ MeV. A dedicated search for such a signal will reassert the bound $g\lesssim 10^{-18}$.

Result: X17粒子在多个独立实验中出现约17 MeV的异常信号，但其存在仍需更高精度的实验验证；理论上该粒子可被解释为轻暗光子或新规范玻色子，可能携带与标准模型费米子的耦合。

### [31] [The $B^+ \to K^+ ν\bar ν$ decay as a QCD axion search: comparing reinterpretation approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20525)
*Merna Abumusabh,Giulio Dujany,Diego Guadagnoli,Méril Reboud,Claudio Toni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了Belle II $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$数据在约束$B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$（QCD轴子）过程中的灵敏度差异来源，发现运动学变量空间的选择（尤其是$q^2_{\rm rec}$的分辨率）是导致约四倍灵敏度差异的主因；BDT变量对$B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$信号鉴别力有限，并建议实验合作组发布物理变量空间上的似然投影以增强测量的可重解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释Belle II $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$数据分析中，对$B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$（轻不可见粒子如QCD轴子）分支比上限存在约四倍差异的原因。

Method: 通过追踪运动学变量空间选择的影响，对比精细与粗糙$q^2_{\rm rec}$分箱对轴子信号分辨率的差异；训练BDT轴并检验其对$B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$的鉴别能力；进行数值测试并考虑次领头阶形状系统误差的影响。

Result: 运动学变量空间选择（$q^2_{\rm rec}$分辨率）是四倍灵敏度差异的唯一原因；BDT变量与$q^2$基本不相关，对轴子信号鉴别力弱；次领头阶形状系统误差实际上降低而非提高轴子信号上限；$q^2_{\rm rec}\timesη({\rm BDT}_2)$空间中的界限显著依赖于$B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$的SM相似度。

Conclusion: 以BDT变量主导的似然函数在信号形状与训练信号差异显著时，可重解释性有限；建议实验合作组在物理变量空间上发布似然投影以最大化测量的可重解释性。

Abstract: Two recent independent analyses of Belle II $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ data yield limits on ${\mathcal B}(B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a)$ -- the two-body mode to a light invisible particle such as the QCD axion -- differing by a factor of roughly four; we trace this to the choice of kinematic variable space. The central figure of merit is the resolution in the reconstructed di-neutrino invariant mass $q^2_{\rm rec}$: fine-grained binning resolves the narrow axion signal, while coarse binning dilutes it into a background-dominated range. A BDT axis trained on $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ adds little discriminating power for $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$, as this axis is largely uncorrelated with $q^2$. These expectations are confirmed by a set of numerical tests. The subleading shape systematics omitted from our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach {\em lower}, not raise, the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ limit: by better accommodating the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ shape, they leave less room for the axion signal, making our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based bound conservative, if anything. A dedicated reanalysis confirms that the kinematic-axes choice alone accounts for the factor-of-four sensitivity difference, and that the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ bound varies sizeably within the $q^2_{\rm rec}\timesη({\rm BDT}_2)$ space, depending on the SM-likeness of $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$, thus losing the dual-probe feature of our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach. These results point to a broader consideration: likelihoods dominated by BDT variables are of limited use for reinterpretations when the signal shape differs appreciably from the BDT's training signal. We therefore advocate that experimental collaborations publish likelihood projections in physical variable spaces alongside BDT-based likelihoods, to maximise the reinterpretability of their measurements.

</details>


### [32] [Rotating magnetized pion gas of finite transverse size: condensation constraints and transport properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20530)
*Ankit Kumar,Diwakar Gaur,Vinod Chandra*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了存在背景磁场时，具有有限横向半径的旋转π介子气体的电、热和热电响应，重点分析了磁场与旋转的竞争效应对输运系数的影响，发现旋转作为有效化学势可以增强输运系数，超越磁场的抑制作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究旋转和磁场共同作用下π介子气体的输运特性，特别是两者之间的竞争机制，以及旋转对磁抑制效应的抵消作用。

Method: 使用玻尔兹曼输运方程在弛豫时间近似下，计算纵向电导率、热导率和塞贝克系数；明确π⁺凝聚的参数边界，确保工作区在边界之外以确保输运系数的良行为。

Result: 1) 系统表现出凝聚不对称性，在诱导π⁺凝聚的参数下π⁻保持未凝聚状态；2) 磁场在静态介质中抑制输运系数，而旋转作为有效化学势引入能量偏移从而增强输运系数；3) 超过某一角速度阈值后，旋转增强效应超过磁抑制，输运系数随磁场增强而增加。

Conclusion: 旋转与磁场对π介子气体输运性质存在竞争关系，旋转可以逆转磁场的抑制作用；通过洛伦兹数分析了电荷与热输运的相对重要性。

Abstract: This work investigates the electric, thermal, and thermoelectric responses of a rotating pion gas of finite transverse radius in the presence of a background magnetic field, with the rotation axis aligned with the magnetic field. We explicitly calculate the parameter limits for $π^+$ condensation and restrict our working regime safely outside these boundaries, ensuring well-behaved transport coefficients. Notably, the system exhibits a condensation asymmetry, with $π^-$ remaining uncondensed at the parameters that induce $π^+$ condensation. Using the Boltzmann Transport Equation under the Relaxation Time Approximation, we calculate the longitudinal electrical conductivity, thermal conductivity, and the Seebeck coefficient. Our results reveal a competing interplay between the magnetic field and rotation, highlighting the substantial impact of rotation on the medium's transport properties: while the magnetic field suppresses the transport coefficients in a static medium, rotation, acting as an effective chemical potential, introduces an energy shift that favors their increase. Beyond an angular velocity, this rotational enhancement overpowers the magnetic suppression, leading to an increase in the transport coefficients with increasing magnetic field. Finally, we analyze the relative significance of charge and heat transport through the Lorenz number, providing further insight into the transport characteristics of the rotating magnetized pion medium.

</details>

### [33] [Exact Solution of the Non-minimally Coupled Klein-Gordon Equation in the Schwarzschild Star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19433)
*Reynan A. Dulinayan,Kevin T. Grosvenor*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次给出了含非最小曲率标量耦合的Klein-Gordon方程在Schwarzschild星（完美流体、均匀密度、球对称星）中的精确解，解以一般Heun函数表示，并通过几何诱导的代数坐标变换揭示了其背后的Fuchsian结构。在低致密极限下恢复了已知的前导和次前导结果；在Buchdahl极限下推导了静态模式的正则性条件，并解析描述了动态模式在接近星体中心压力奇异性时振幅和振荡波矢的发散行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前缺乏含非最小曲率标量耦合的Klein-Gordon方程在致密星内部（特别是Schwarzschild星）的精确解，现有研究多局限于低致密近似或忽略非最小耦合，无法完整描述Buchdahl极限附近的物理行为。

Method: 通过几何诱导的代数坐标变换将方程转化为Fuchs型微分方程，进而利用一般Heun函数表达精确解。

Result: 得到了含非最小耦合项的Klein-Gordon方程在均匀密度球对称星内的精确解；在低致密极限下复现了已知微扰结果；在Buchdahl极限下得到了静态模式的正则性条件，并解析描述了动态模式在中心奇点处的振幅发散和波矢振荡行为。

Conclusion: 该精确解为研究致密天体内部标量场动力学提供了完整框架，特别有助于理解Buchdahl极限附近标量场的奇异性行为及非最小耦合效应。

Abstract: We present for the first time the exact solution of the massive Klein-Gordon equation in the Schwarzschild star (perfect-fluid, uniform-density, spherically-symmetric star), including the non-minimal curvature-scalar coupling. The solution is expressed in terms of the general Heun function. A geometry-induced algebraic coordinate transformation reveals a hidden Fuchsian structure that underlies the exact solvability. Known leading- and next-to-leading-order results are recovered in the low-compactness limit. In the Buchdahl limit, we derive a regularity condition for static modes and describe analytically the divergence in amplitude and oscillation wave vector of dynamic modes as they approach the pressure singularity at the center of the star.

</details>


### [34] [Deriving effective descriptions and signal predictions for dynamical gravitational systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19435)
*Steven B. Giddings,Madhur Mehta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于腔边界有效作用量来描述引力系统（如双星）辐射的顶向下推导方法，通过边界腔体描述替代传统世界线有效场论，以解决截断依赖问题，并展示了如何将腔体描述与可观测物理量（波形、相移）关联，特别关注修改经典黑洞行为对引力波信号的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主要动机是建立一种系统性的方法来推断经典黑洞行为的修改（例如出于量子力学一致性要求的黑洞演化修正，或其他新物理模型）对引力波信号的影响。特别地，累积相位偏移被认为对旋近阶段的小效应具有敏感性。

Method: 采用顶向下推导方法，基于边界腔体（cavity）上的作用量来参数化动力学，替代传统世界线有效场论（worldline EFT）。为黑洞和修正黑洞行为的简单模型给出了腔体描述示例，并通过标量辐射示例阐明原理，随后概述向引力波背景的扩展。

Result: 给出了黑洞及修正黑洞模型的腔体描述示例，展示了腔体有效描述如何连接可观测物理量（详细波形和累积相位偏移）。

Conclusion: 腔体有效描述为解决世界线EFT中的截断依赖问题提供了替代方案，可系统性地将修改黑洞行为的新物理效应与引力波可观测信号关联起来，为探测量子引力等新物理提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate top-down derivations of effective descriptions for radiation from gravitational systems such as binaries. With a specified cutoff prescription, one can derive worldline effective field theories, but the cutoff dependence also complicates their description. We investigate a related effective approach, based on parameterizing dynamics in terms of an action on the boundaries of cavities encompassing individual bodies. We give examples of such cavity descriptions for black holes and for simple models for modifications of their behavior. We also show how cavity effective descriptions connect to observable quantities -- detailed wave profiles, and importantly, accumulated phase shift of emitted signals. A primary motivation is to have a systematic approach to inferring effects of modification of classical black hole behavior, such as those motivated by the need for black hole evolution to be consistent with quantum mechanics, or by other models for new BH behavior, on gravitational wave signals; the latter phase shifts have in particular been argued to provide sensitivity to small new effects from the inspiral phase. To illustrate basic principles and methods, this paper largely focuses on examples with scalar radiation, but we outline extension of the analysis to gravitational wave contexts.

### [35] [Dynamical Tidal Response of Neutron Stars: from Effective Field Theory to Gravitational Waveforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19446)
*Thomas Apostolidis,Valerio De Luca,Leonardo Gualtieri,Takuya Katagiri,Paolo Pani,Luca Santoni*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在完全相对论框架下研究了中子星的动力学潮汐响应（含二阶频修正），通过世界线有效场论与相对论恒星模型摄动理论的匹配，首次推导了完整领头阶动力学潮汐修正对致密双星保守动力学和引力波信号的影响，并发现动力学效应不能仅由模式激发完全描述，其贡献虽在8阶后牛顿序进入引力波相位，但在晚期旋进中不可忽略，第三代探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）有望测量动力学Love数，忽略则会导致静态Love数及核物质状态方程推断的显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波模型多采用静态潮汐Love数近似，而实际双星旋进过程中潮汐场是时变的，动力学潮汐效应在相对论框架下尚缺乏系统、完整的领头阶修正计算，特别是包含普适对数跑动项及格式依赖有限项的一致性处理。

Method: 结合世界线有效场论（EFT）与相对论恒星模型的线性摄动理论，采用维数正规化方案，通过一致性匹配流程推导外时变场诱导的动力学潮汐形变，分析二阶频修正下的动力学Love数表达及其与恒星致密度、状态方程和跑动项的关系。

Result: 动力学Love数在小致密度下显著增强；动力学效应对引力波相位的贡献虽形式上是8阶后牛顿序，但在晚期旋进中不可忽略；Fisher矩阵分析表明第三代探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）可测量动力学Love数；忽略动力学效应将导致静态Love数及核状态方程推断的显著偏差。

Conclusion: 动力学潮汐效应对于未来高精度引力波建模至关重要，必须纳入模型以避免对中子星状态方程的错误推断。

Abstract: We investigate the fully relativistic dynamical tidal response of neutron stars up to second order in the frequency. Combining the worldline effective field theory for extended gravitating bodies with perturbation theory of relativistic stellar models, we derive the tidal deformation induced by an external time-dependent field, including a universal logarithmic running term. In the effective theory, we work in dimensional regularization and, through a consistent matching procedure, obtain for the first time the complete leading-order dynamical tidal corrections to both the conservative dynamics and the gravitational-wave signal of compact binaries, including the scheme-dependent finite terms in addition to the running. We show that, in the relativistic regime, dynamical effects cannot be fully captured by mode excitations alone. The magnitude of the additional contribution depends on the stellar compactness, the equation of state, and the running term. Dynamical Love numbers are significantly enhanced with respect to their static counterparts for relatively small compactness. As a result, although they formally enter the gravitational-wave phase at 8th post-Newtonian order, dynamical tidal effects yield a non-negligible contribution during the late inspiral. Using a Fisher-matrix analysis, we show that third-generation detectors such as the Einstein Telescope could measure dynamical Love numbers for a range of neutron-star masses and equations of state. Conversely, neglecting these effects can lead to significant biases in the inference of static Love numbers, and hence on the nuclear equation of state. Our results highlight the importance of dynamical tidal effects for high-precision gravitational-wave modeling with future detectors.

</details>

Method: 在FLRW度规下引入q-形变耦合函数，推导广义Friedmann方程；通过求解无物质情形下的精确解析解，将标量场贡献等效为理想流体，并计算状态方程参数和减速参数。

In the matter-free sector, we obtain exact analytic solutions for the scale factor and the Brans-Dicke scalar field, and recast the scalar contribution as an effective fluid. We show that the corresponding equation-of-state parameter and the deceleration parameter are constants and depend only on the Brans-Dicke coupling $ω$ and the deformation function, allowing the scalar sector to mimic radiation-, matter-, or dark-energy-like behavior for a restricted region of parameter space.

In particular, we consider polarization-dependent modifications to photon trajectories induced by higher-order curvature terms and analyze their effects in static and spherically symmetric spacetimes, focusing on Schwarzschild and Reissner-Nordström backgrounds.
  Using the geometrical optics approximation, we derive the effective metric governing photon propagation and study the resulting shifts in the photon sphere. ### [39] [Photon surfaces extension in general spherical dust collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19809)
*Roberto Giambò,Camilla Lucamarini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将光球面分析从边缘束缚情况推广到一般（非边缘束缚）LTB尘埃坍缩模型。通过发展非自治一阶动力系统，证明外部光子球面r=3M进入坍缩尘埃云时唯一物理可接受的延伸是零超曲面，且该光球面到达中心奇点当且仅当奇点是裸的，从而将已知结论推广至一般情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从LTB度规出发，在k(x)≠0条件下推导光球面方程，将类时超曲面成为光球面的几何条件重新表述为非自治一阶动力系统；利用文献中已有的隐式解和常微分方程比较定理进行定性分析；结合一般LTB模型的因果结构研究光球面与中心奇点的关系。

Conclusion: 光球面动力学与奇点裸性之间的等价关系在一般LTB模型中成立，这进一步支持了裸奇点与覆盖奇点在光球面行为上的结构二分法，并可能与黑洞阴影的早期演化观测信号相关联。

Abstract: We extend the analysis of photon surfaces in spherical dust collapse to the general, non-marginally bound case, i.e.\ allowing the \textit{energy function} $k(x)$ of the Lemaître--Tolman--Bondi (LTB) model to be non-zero. Starting from the dynamical-systems formulation developed in our previous work for the marginally bound case (arXiv:2509.01368), we derive the photon surface equations for the LTB metric with $k(x)\neq 0$, and we recast the geometric condition for a timelike hypersurface to be a photon surface as a non-autonomous first-order dynamical system. Even though the LTB evolution equation does not integrate in closed form when $k(x)\neq 0$, the implicit solutions available in the literature, together with comparison theorems for ordinary differential equations, are sufficient to show that the only physically acceptable extension of the exterior photon sphere $r=3M$ into the collapsing dust cloud is a null hypersurface, generated by outgoing radial null geodesics. Combining this fact with the known results on the causal structure of the general LTB model, we then establish that the photon surface reaches the central singularity if and only if the singularity is naked, thereby extending to the general case the picture already known in the marginally bound regime. The structural dichotomy between the naked and covered end states is also discussed in connection with possible observational signatures in the early-time evolution of black-hole shadows.

### [40] [Covariant Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations in Energy-Momentum Squared Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19879)
*Eduardo Bittencourt,Mariam Campbell,Peter K. S. Dunsby,Sergio E. Jorás*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在能量-动量平方引力框架下，利用协变1+1+2半-tetrad形式体系，研究了静态球对称恒星结构。通过将非线性物质修正重新解释为有效完美流体，恒星平衡方程保持Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff形式。在存在有效闭合关系时，方程可约化为自治平面动力系统，揭示了恒星相空间的全局定性结构。在线性物态方程下，识别了与广义相对论精确、渐近或分段等价的扇区，以及平面约化失效的情形（如尘埃组态）。还表明外部时空仍为Schwarzschild，但恒星表面的自然匹配条件为p_eff(R)=0，不一定等于p(R)=0。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将广义相对论扩展到能量-动量平方引力框架，研究非线性物质修正对致密恒星结构的影响，并发展适用于该理论的恒星平衡方程协变形式体系。

Method: 采用协变1+1+2半-tetrad形式体系，将非线性物质修正重新解释为有效完美流体，导出有效变量的TOV方程；通过平面动力系统分析相空间全局结构，并讨论尘埃组态等特殊情形下的三维协变流。

Result: 证明了非线性物质修正可映射为有效完美流体，平衡方程保持TOV形式；外部时空仍为Schwarzschild，但表面匹配条件为p_eff(R)=0而非p(R)=0；线性物态方程下存在与GR精确、渐近或分段等价的扇区，尘埃组态需处理三维流。

Conclusion: 能量-动量平方引力中的恒星结构可通过有效变量简化为标准TOV形式，但表面匹配条件与GR不同（自束缚物质边界处物理压强可非零），且系统在某些扇区（如尘埃）中无法降维，需完整的三维分析。

Abstract: We study static, spherically symmetric stellar configurations in an extended class of Energy--Momentum Squared Gravity using the covariant \(1+1+2\) semi-tetrad formalism. For perfect physical fluids, we show that the nonlinear matter corrections can be reinterpreted as an effective perfect fluid, so that the stellar equilibrium equations retain the standard Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff form when written in terms of effective variables. The resulting covariant structure equations are formulated in both metric and dimensionless variables and, whenever an effective closure relation exists, reduce to an autonomous planar dynamical system. This provides a global qualitative description of the stellar phase space in terms of finite and asymptotic critical points.
  Specializing to linear physical equations of state, we recover the general relativistic benchmark and identify sectors that are exactly, asymptotically, or piecewise equivalent to general relativity, as well as sectors -- particularly dust configurations -- for which the planar reduction breaks down and the full three-dimensional covariant flow must be considered. We further recover the standard metric Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff equation in terms of effective variables and show that, although the exterior spacetime remains Schwarzschild, the natural matching condition at the stellar surface is \(p_{\rm eff}(R)=0\), which need not coincide with \(p(R)=0\) for self-bound matter.

### [41] [Cosmological Constraints on Minimal Cubic Galileon Models in Teleparallel Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19905)
*Akbar Davlataliev,Abdurakhmon Nosirov,Odil Yunusov,Bobomurat Ahmedov,Jackson Levi Said*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在teleparallel引力框架下研究了三次Galileon宇宙学模型，利用Pantheon⁺、宇宙时钟、SH0ES和BAO数据对二次和指数势的四种场景进行观测约束。发现固定b₁的二次势模型在包含BAO数据时拟合最优，其χ²最小值低于ΛCDM，但BIC准则仍偏好ΛCDM，表明模型在现象学上可行但需进一步检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越ΛCDM范式，在teleparallel引力框架下探索三次Galileon模型解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀的可行性，并考察不同势函数和模型参数b₁对观测拟合的影响。

Method: 在teleparallel引力框架中构建三次Galileon模型，通过参数b₁编码对标准对等引力的偏离；考虑二次势和指数势两种标量场势函数，设定b₁自由和b₁=2固定共四种场景；使用Pantheon⁺ Ia型超新星样本、宇宙时钟测量、SH0ES信息和重子声学振荡数据进行参数约束和模型比较。

Result: 固定b₁的二次势模型在包含BAO数据时拟合最优，χ²最小值低于ΛCDM，AIC准则给出可比支持；但BIC准则仍偏好ΛCDM，因扩展模型参数空间更大。所有模型都能描述晚期膨胀历史，统计偏好取决于势函数选择和b₁是否自由。

Conclusion: Teleparallel三次Galileon宇宙学在现象学上可行，但尚无法在模型选择层面明确优于ΛCDM；对哈勃张力的更强声明需要更多一致性检验。

Abstract: Cubic Galileon cosmological models provide a well-motivated framework for investigating late-time cosmic acceleration beyond the standard $Λ$CDM paradigm. In this work, we study observational constraints on cubic Galileon models within the teleparallel gravity framework, where deviations from the standard teleparallel equivalent of general relativity are encoded through the model parameter $b_1$. We consider two scalar-field potentials, namely quadratic and exponential potentials, and analyze four representative scenarios: quadratic and exponential potentials with $b_1$ treated as a free parameter, together with the corresponding cases in which $b_1=2$ is fixed. Using the $\text{Pantheon}^+$ Type Ia supernova sample, cosmic chronometer measurements, SH0ES information, and baryon acoustic oscillation data, we constrain the cosmological and model parameters and compare the observational viability of the different scenarios. We find that the considered teleparallel cubic Galileon models can accommodate the late-time expansion history, although the statistical preference depends on the choice of potential and on whether $b_1$ is fixed or varied. In particular, the fixed-$b_1$ model with a quadratic potential provides the most competitive fit among the Galileon scenarios when BAO data are included, showing a lower $χ^2_{\min}$ than $Λ$CDM and comparable support according to the AIC criterion. However, the BIC criterion continues to favor the minimal $Λ$CDM model because of the larger parameter space of the extended models. These results suggest that teleparallel cubic Galileon cosmologies remain phenomenologically viable, while a stronger claim regarding the Hubble tension requires further consistency tests.

</details>


### [42] [On the Plebanski Formulation with Energy Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20042)
*Jack C. M. Hughes,Joudy F. Jamal Beek,Fedor V. Kusmartsev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将能量-动量张量系统地映射到Plebanski形式中自对偶/反自对偶物质源项的方法，并使用Kulkarni-Nomizu积和手征分解构造了物质源T^i，验证了场方程与守恒律的一致性，并以电磁应力-能量张量为例导出了Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Plebanski形式中物质耦合不如度规形式直接，因为能量-动量张量是对称的，而Plebanski变量自然取值于2-形式的自对偶/反自对偶Hodge分解中，需要建立从度规物质源到Plebanski物质源的系统映射。

Method: 通过Kulkarni-Nomizu积将无迹能量-动量张量提升到代数曲率空间的(1,1)分量，再提取其手征分量来构造Plebanski物质源T^i；利用手征Bianchi恒等式验证了耦合场方程蕴含守恒律；将方法应用于球对称电磁应力-能量张量。

Result: 该构造重现了Krasnov用自对偶基Σ^i和能量-动量张量定义T^i的表达式；验证了手征Bianchi恒等式d^A F^i=0保证能量-动量守恒；应用于球对称电磁场时得到Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter解。

Conclusion: 该工作为将度规物质源系统地翻译为Plebanski场方程所需的反自对偶源项提供了规范化的处方。

Abstract: In Plebanski's formulation the coupling of matter is less direct than in the metric formulation since the energy-momentum tensor $T_{μν}$ is symmetric, while the Plebanski variables are naturally valued in the self-dual/anti-self-dual Hodge decomposition of 2-forms. An explicit construction of the Plebanski matter source $T^i$ is obtained by lifting the trace-free energy-momentum tensor $\hat T_{μν}$ into the $(1,1)$ component of the algebraic curvature space using the Kulkarni-Nomizu product, and then extracting its chiral components. This construction reproduces the definition for $T^i$ in terms of the self-dual basis $Σ^i$ and $\hat T_{μν}$ introduced by Krasnov. We also verify that the matter-coupled chiral field equations imply the usual conservation law $\nabla_μT^{μν}=0$ through the chiral Bianchi identity $d^A F^i=0$. As an application, the construction is applied to a spherically symmetric electromagnetic stress-energy tensor, where the anti-self-dual part of the matter-coupled Plebanski field equations yields the Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter solution. The result gives a systematic prescription for translating metric matter sources into the anti-self-dual source terms required by the Plebanski field equations.

</details>


### [43] [Regular Black Holes from Anisotropic Source with Hydrodynamic Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20109)
*Hassan Firouzjahi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究各向异性能动张量源生的规则黑洞解，通过假设流体力学状态方程P=P(ρ)导出新的度规，发现声速平方在P最大值处变号（潜在不稳定性），亚光速条件排除指数衰减模型，并建立了强能量条件破坏、P的根与最大值之间的普适层级关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究各向异性源下规则黑洞解的普遍性质，特别是状态方程P(ρ)的轮廓特征及其对稳定性的影响。

Method: 将能动张量分解为各向同性与各向异性分量，假设流体力学状态方程P=P(ρ)，求解球对称规则黑洞解，分析声速平方和能量条件。

Result: P(ρ)在远距离趋近0⁺时存在根和极大值；c_s²在极大值处变号表明潜在流体力学不稳定性；亚光速条件排除指数衰减能密度模型；建立了SEC破坏点、P的根与极大值之间的普适层级关系。

Conclusion: 规则黑洞的状态方程P(ρ)的轮廓性质决定了其稳定性与参数约束，不同P(ρ)形式可统一现有和新解。

Abstract: We study regular black hole solutions sourced by an anisotropic energy momentum tensor. It is well known that the geometry of the interior of a spherically symmetric regular black hole approaches the dS metric. Having decomposed the energy momentum tensor into its isotropic and anisotropic components, we assume a hydrodynamic equation of state, $P= P(ρ)$, for the pressure, and look for spherically symmetric, regular black hole solutions. We consider different forms of $ P(ρ)$ which yield the previously known regular black hole solutions, as well as various new metrics. We show that the profile of $ P(ρ)$ has a root and a maximum as it approaches $0^+$ at large distances. Consequently, the square of the sound speed of perturbations, $c_s^2$, changes sign at the point where $P$ reaches its maximum, indicating a potential hydrodynamic instability. In addition, imposing the subluminal bound on $c_s$ puts strong constraints on the model parameters, excluding models in which the energy density has an exponential fall off. We establish a universal hierarchy among the relative positions at which the strong energy condition is violated, at which $P$ has its root, and at which $P$ attains its maximum.

### [44] [The auxiliary-metric formulation of Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20247)
*Bayram Tekin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入辅助度规将Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity (BINMG)重新表述为多项式形式，简化了其性质推导，证明了其在AdS背景上的电荷、质量、角动量等物理量均为Einstein结果乘以共同因子，并隔离了非线性自由度问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: New Massive Gravity通过曲率无穷级数推广到所有阶得到BINMG，但原始形式代数复杂。本文动机是寻找一个更简洁的表述，简化其性质推导并隔离自由度问题。

Method: 引入独立辅助度规 q_{μν}，其代数运动方程 q_{μν}=g_{μν}+(σ/m²)G_{μν}(g) 精确恢复行列式作用量。使用密化变量 P^{μν}=√(-q) q^{μν} 使三维作用量变为多项式形式，所有导数依赖由耦合项 P^{μν}G_{μν}(g) 承载。

Result: 唯一真空一行导出；二次作用量给出单个Pauli-Fierz有质量自旋-2场，Fierz-Pauli调谐自然产生而非人为施加；在局部AdS背景上，守恒荷、BTZ质量和角动量、中心荷、熵均简化为Einstein结果乘以共同因子。

Conclusion: 新表述显著简化了BINMG的代数处理，揭示了其与Einstein引力的比例关系，并为完整的Dirac自由度计数分析奠定了基础。

Abstract: Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity (BINMG) completes New Massive Gravity to all orders in curvature through the determinant of the metric shifted by the Einstein tensor. We recast it with an independent auxiliary metric $q_{μν}$, whose algebraic equation of motion $q_{μν}=g_{μν}+\fracσ{m^2}G_{μν}(g)$ recovers the determinant action exactly on the regular branch and resums the infinite curvature series into a single relation. In the densitized variable $P^{μν}=\sqrt{-q}\,q^{μν}$ the three-dimensional action is polynomial, with all derivative dependence carried by the coupling $P^{μν}G_{μν}(g)$. The formulation makes known properties follow with substantially less algebra: the unique vacuum follows in one line, and the quadratic action yields a single Pauli-Fierz massive spin-2 field with the Fierz-Pauli tuning generated rather than imposed. On locally AdS backgrounds the conserved charges, BTZ mass and angular momentum, central charge, and entropy reduce to the Einstein results times a common factor. The formulation also isolates the nonlinear degree-of-freedom problem in the right variables, leaving the full Dirac count to separate work.

</details>


### [45] [An explicit and differentiable Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer transform for gravitational-wave data analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20269)
*Avi Vajpeyi,Giorgio Mentasti,Quentin Baghi,Ollie Burke,Lorenzo Speri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个开源的Python包wdm_transform，实现了Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer (WDM) 时频变换，支持NumPy和JAX后端，可在数十毫秒内对百万点数据流进行GPU加速变换。通过LISA银河双星案例验证了WDM域似然与频域后验的数值等价性，为未来引力波探测中的非平稳噪声、随机背景和数据间隙处理提供了新工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: WDM时频变换在引力波天文学中已被广泛使用，但缺乏一个自包含、数学上明确且面向实践的参考文档，尤其是在现代Python和JAX推理工作流中的应用需求日益增长。

Method: 开发了wdm_transform Python包，实现WDM小波包时频变换的前向和逆向变换，提供NumPy和JAX双后端支持，并验证其浮点精度；通过LISA银河双星案例检验WDM域似然与频域后验的一致性。

Result: JAX后端可在数十毫秒内完成百万点数据流的GPU加速变换；在共享平稳噪声模型下，WDM域似然与频域后验具有数值等价性。

Conclusion: 该工作为WDM时频网格的系统优化铺平了道路，适用于未来探测器中的非平稳噪声、随机背景和数据间隙等挑战，并支持与其他时频表示的直接比较。

Abstract: The Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer (WDM) time-frequency transform has been widely used in gravitational-wave astronomy, yet a self-contained, mathematically explicit reference for practitioners remains lacking. This is especially true for those wishing to adopt the transform in modern Python and JAX inference workflows. We present wdm_transform, an open-source Python package implementing the WDM wavelet-packet time-frequency transform, and document its mathematical foundations, statistical properties, and practical implementation for gravitational-wave data analysis. The package supplies NumPy and JAX backends, both transforms (forward and inverse) validated to floating-point precision, with the JAX backend enabling GPU-accelerated transforms of million-point data streams in tens of milliseconds. As a worked example, we verify that the WDM-domain likelihood reproduces frequency-domain posteriors for a resolved LISA galactic binary under a shared stationary noise model, confirming numerical equivalence of the two representations in that controlled setting. This work paves the way for systematic optimisation of WDM tilings, a particularly promising direction for the non-stationary noise, stochastic backgrounds, and data gaps anticipated in future detectors, and for direct comparisons with alternative time-frequency representations needed to meet the challenges of future gravitational-wave data analysis.

### [46] [Constitutive birefringence and critical curves in the rotating García--Díaz black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20284)
*Ariel Guzmán,Mohsen Fathi,J. R. Villanueva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究旋转García–Díaz解中高频电磁波在非线性电动力学（NLED）耦合引力系统中的传播。NLED场作为光学介质，导致物理光锥偏离时空度规零锥。通过混合电磁势投影到主标架得到标量，重建局部本构分支，进而导出两个光学度规。两个光学度规均允许Carter型分离，并产生两个临界轮廓Γ+和Γ−，在麦克斯韦极限下重合，在非线性响应激活时分裂。通过最大角分离、相对直径偏移和归一化双折射宽度量化分裂，展示了局部NLED响应与偏振依赖临界结构之间的直接几何联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非线性电动力学（NLED）耦合引力系统中高频电磁传播的行为，特别是NLED场作为光学介质对光锥结构的影响，以及这种影响如何在天体观测中表现为可量化的双折射效应。

Method: 将电磁场F和激发P投影到主标架上获得对齐标量E、B、D、H，重建规则局部本构分支；将响应矩阵代入Fresnel特征问题，对Fresnel四次型进行因式分解得到两个二次分支（即两个光学度规）；对光学度规进行Hamilton-Jacobi方程的Carter型分离，求解临界常数和临界轨道族，并将临界族投影到有限距离观测者的天球上。

Result: 两个光学度规各自拥有独立的径向和角度势、临界常数和不稳定临界族，产生两个临界轮廓Γ+和Γ−。在麦克斯韦极限下两轮廓重合，非线性响应激活时发生分裂。通过数值扫描发现分裂由本构响应产生，受旋转重新分布，且在微扰域内对局部投影变化保持稳定。

Conclusion: 建立了局部NLED响应与观测者屏幕上偏振依赖临界结构之间的直接几何联系，为通过天体观测检验非线性电动力学效应提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We study high-frequency electromagnetic propagation in the rotating García--Díaz solution of Einstein gravity coupled to NLED. In this system, light is not governed only by the null cone of the spacetime metric, because the NLED field also behaves as an optical medium whose constitutive response determines the physical optical cones. Starting from the mixed electromagnetic potentials, we project the field $F$ and the excitation $P$ on a principal tetrad and obtain the aligned scalars $E$, $B$, $D$ and $H$. These scalars allow us to reconstruct the regular local constitutive branch connected with Maxwell theory through the map $(D,B)\mapsto(E,H)$. We then insert the resulting response matrix into the Fresnel characteristic problem. At the perturbative order considered here, the Fresnel quartic factorizes into two quadratic branches, each defining an effective optical metric. Both optical metrics admit Carter-type separation of the Hamilton--Jacobi equation and possess their own radial and angular potentials, critical constants and unstable critical families. By projecting these families onto the celestial sphere of a finite-distance observer, we obtain two critical contours, $Γ_+$ and $Γ_-$, which coincide in the Maxwell limit and split when the nonlinear constitutive response is active. We quantify this birefringent splitting through the maximum angular separation, the relative diameter shift and the normalized birefringent width. Numerical scans over the nonlinear coupling, spin and observer inclination show that the splitting is generated by the constitutive response, redistributed by rotation and stable under local projection changes within the perturbative domain. This provides a direct geometrical link between the local NLED response and a polarization-dependent critical structure on the observer screen.

Abstract: In PRL 129, 110401 it was shown that it is theoretically possible to have operationally detectable causal loops without violating the principle of no superluminal signalling (NSS) in (1+1)-Minkowski spacetime. Whether or not such causal loops are also possible in $d > 1$ spatial dimensions, has remained a key open question. We resolve this question by showing that in a wide class of "conical" spacetimes, including Minkowski with d > 1, NSS does rule out all operationally detectable causal loops, in classical, quantum and post-quantum theories. This establishes that the relationship between the relativistic principles of NSS and no causal loops depends inherently on the geometry of spacetime.

### [49] [Higher Lovelock Curvature Terms Favor Local Nakedness in Dust Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20540)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过解析分析球对称尘埃塌缩模型，考虑最高非零Lovelock阶数N的影响，研究非临界维度（D-1-2N>0）和临界维度（D=2N+1）两种情况下的表观视界形成与奇点曲线行为。

Conclusion: 高阶Lovelock项不仅不能恢复局部宇宙监察，反而促进了奇点的局部可见性。可见奇点沿出射零射线为Królak强奇点，在阈值处达到Tipler强度。

Abstract: We show that higher-curvature Lovelock terms do not restore local cosmic censorship in spherical dust collapse, but instead promote the local visibility of central shell-focusing singularities. On the collapse branch with positive highest-order Lovelock coefficient \(c_N\), the highest nonvanishing Lovelock order \(N\) controls both the near-singularity collapse and the formation of trapped surfaces. In noncritical dimensions, \(D-1-2N>0\), the apparent-horizon curve approaches the singularity curve with trapping exponent \(β_N=(D-1)/(D-1-2N)\). Comparing this scale with the first nonvanishing correction \(r^\ell\) to the singularity curve gives the local-visibility condition \(\ell<β_N\), provided the singularity curve opens outward. Thus increasing \(N\) enlarges the class of inhomogeneous initial data producing outgoing radial null rays from the central singularity. In the critical odd-dimensional branch, \(D=2N+1\), no apparent horizon forms sufficiently close to the center, so any outward opening of the singularity curve gives local visibility. The locally visible singularities are Królak-strong along the emerging null rays, with Tipler strength reached at threshold. For bound and unbound collapse, the noncritical exponents are unchanged: the energy function modifies the opening of the singularity curve, while in the critical branch it enters the leading terminal collapse velocity.

</details>

### [50] [Bootstrapping Pion Form Factors at Large $N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19420)
*Jan Albert,Dilara Kosva,Leonardo Rastelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过大N QCD中的自举方法研究π介子形状因子，结合解析性、幺正性、Regge行为及Brodsky-Farrar标度律，得到两类约束：一类是严格的低能形状因子系数界限，另一类是类似SVZ求和规则的唯象界限，约束了π介子衰变常数、手征拉氏量空间及渐近自由标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大N极限下，QCD可观测量退化为亚纯函数，为自举研究提供了严格的解析结构。作者希望利用这种结构，结合强子自举方法与微扰QCD，建立从低能手征有效理论到高能渐近自由之间的桥梁。

Method: 采用大N QCD自举方法，研究矢量流两点函数、π介子矢量形状因子和π介子散射振幅构成的混合系统。利用解析性、幺正性、交叉对称性和Regge有界性作为约束条件，分别引入Brodsky-Farrar渐近标度律（第一类严格约束）和有限能标下的微扰紫外行为（第二类SVZ型唯象约束）。

Result: 获得了低能形状因子系数的严格界限；通过输入微扰紫外行为，约束了π介子衰变常数、π介子电荷半径，并将大N格点测量转换为渐近自由标度的下界；手征拉氏量的允许空间被显著压缩至大N QCD预期区域。

Conclusion: 局域规范不变探针为强子自举与微观QCD拉氏量之间提供了规范桥梁，验证了自举方法在大N QCD中的有效性，并展示了如何从第一性原理出发约束低能强子物理参数。

Abstract: We initiate a bootstrap study of pion form factors in large $N$ QCD. We consider the mixed system of the vector-current two-point function, the pion vector form factor, and the pion scattering amplitude in the chiral limit. At large $N$ these observables are meromorphic, with spectral data constrained by unitarity, crossing symmetry, and Regge boundedness. We obtain bounds of two kinds. The first are rigorous and universal: from analyticity, unitarity and the asymptotic Brodsky-Farrar scaling, we constrain low-energy form-factor coefficients. The second are more phenomenological, of the Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov type: feeding in the perturbative ultraviolet behavior at a finite scale lets us bound the pion decay constant, convert a large $N$ lattice measurement into a lower bound on the scale at which asymptotic freedom sets in, and constrain the pion charge radius. Combining these inputs, the space of allowed chiral Lagrangians shrinks toward the region where large $N$ QCD is expected to sit. Our results illustrate how local gauge-invariant probes provide a canonical bridge between the hadronic bootstrap and the microscopic QCD Lagrangian.
