Conclusion: Frontier解码器在稀疏量子解码中兼顾了高性能与低复杂度，其线性复杂度特性为低延迟量子纠错实现提供了可能，有望推动实用化量子计算的纠错方案发展。

Abstract: We introduce the Frontier decoder, a pruned dynamic-programming decoder for sparse quantum decoding problems. Frontier processes error variables in a chosen order, merges prefixes with the same residual syndrome and logical label, and approximates logical-coset posterior masses by retaining only a narrow scored frontier. Without pruning, the recursion is exact ordered inference with exponential complexity.
  In the code-capacity setting, the decoder reaches thresholds close to optimal for the surface code and the color code. In the circuit-level noise model, it achieves state-of-the-art performance with a very small average retained list size: less than 100 for the gross code $[[144,12,12]]$ at a physical error rate of $0.001$. When the list size is constant, the decoder has linear complexity, suggesting the possibility of low-latency implementations.

*Emanuel-Cristian Boghiu,Kyrylo Simonov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究因果顺序不确定场景下的Guess-Your-Neighbour's-Input博弈，通过GPU加速的半定规划方法探索局部维度d=5至8的策略空间，发现d=5已接近最优，未能在更高维度取得显著提升，表明要么需要全新策略来逼近已知上界0.7592，要么该上界本身不紧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缩小Guess-Your-Neighbour's-Input博弈中已知最优策略（d=5时约0.6218）与最强维度无关上界（0.7592）之间的差距，探究增加局部维度是否能提升获胜概率。

Method: 采用see-saw优化方案，每步建模为半定规划（SDP）；为提升可扩展性，开发了SCS求解器的定制实现，将主要计算成本——正半定锥投影——卸载至GPU，获得六倍加速。利用该实现探索d=5至8的局部维度。

Result: 局部维度从d=5提升至d=8并未带来获胜概率的显著改善。

Conclusion: 要么需要定性不同的策略才能逼近已知上界0.7592，要么该上界本身并非紧致（即可能不严格）。

Abstract: The process matrix formalism describes quantum correlations in scenarios without a fixed causal order between local laboratories. Operational signatures of such correlations can be investigated through causal games. A paradigmatic example is the Guess-Your-Neighbour's-Input game, in which two parties attempt to guess each other's inputs. Correlations compatible with any definite, or probabilistically mixed, causal order cannot achieve a winning probability exceeding $1/2$. The best process-matrix strategy currently known attains a value of approximately $0.6218$ using local dimension $d=5$, while the strongest known dimension-independent upper bound is $0.7592$. In this work, we investigate whether increasing the local dimension beyond $d = 5$ can narrow this gap. To this end, we employ a see-saw optimization scheme in which each step is formulated as a semidefinite program. For scalability, we develop a custom implementation of the SCS solver in which the dominant computational cost, the projection onto the positive-semidefinite cone, is offloaded to a GPU, yielding a six-fold speedup. Using this implementation, we explore local dimensions up to $d = 8$, and we do not find significant improvements over the value at $d=5$. Our results suggest that either qualitatively different strategies are required to approach the known upper bound, or that the bound itself is not tight.

### [134] [Near-Optimal Learning of Local Lindbladians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20535)
*Itai Arad,Zhili Chen,Naixu Guo,Patrick Rebentrost,Zhan Yu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究从黑箱动力学中学习局部林德布拉德算符的问题，提出了一种基于有限时间通道探测、经典阴影和局部傅里叶逆变换的算法，能以近乎最优的采样复杂度和演化时间估计哈密顿量与耗散系数，并给出了匹配的下界，证明在存在耗散时无法达到海森堡极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从黑箱物理演化中学习局部林德布拉德算符（包括哈密顿量和耗散系数），填补开放量子系统学习理论中关于局部耗散系数可学习性的空白，并探究耗散存在时海森堡极限是否可达。

Method: 算法直接基于有限时间通道探测：短时间运行未知演化，通过经典阴影估计对应泡利转移矩阵，再通过稳定的局部傅里叶逆变换将估计值转换为林德布拉德系数。算法非自适应、无需辅助比特，仅使用随机乘积态作为输入并执行随机泡利测量。

Result: 在固定局域性和有界耗散位点度下，动力学调用次数为$\widetilde{O}(Λ^2/\varepsilon^2)$，总演化时间为$\widetilde{O}(Λ/\varepsilon^2)$，对量子比特数仅对数依赖。同时给出匹配下界：构造了单量子比特退相位林德布拉德族，对自适应算法仍需$Ω(Λ^2/\varepsilon^2)$通道使用和$Ω(Λ/\varepsilon^2)$总演化时间，证明耗散系数存在时哈密顿学习中的海森堡极限不可达。

Conclusion: 该算法在采样复杂度和总演化时间上均达到近乎最优，且揭示了耗散存在从根本上改变了开放量子系统学习的复杂度标度——信息论意义上无法实现海森堡极限。

Abstract: We study the problem of learning local Lindbladians from black-box access to the physical evolution, and the goal is to estimate all Hamiltonian and dissipative coefficients. We give an algorithm built directly from finite-time channel probes, which runs the unknown evolution for short times, estimates the corresponding Pauli transfer matrices from classical shadows, and converts these estimates into Lindbladian coefficients by stable local Fourier inversions. For fixed locality and bounded dissipative site degree, the uses of the dynamical evolution and total evolution time scale as $\widetilde{O}(Λ^2/\varepsilon^2)$ and $\widetilde{O}(Λ/\varepsilon^2)$ respectively, in the local dynamical strength bound $Λ$ and target accuracy $\varepsilon$, with only logarithmic dependence on the number of qubits. The algorithm is non-adaptive, uses no ancillas, and uses only random product states as inputs followed by random Pauli measurements. The method does not require knowing the support of the Lindbladian in advance. We complement the algorithm with matching lower bounds, showing that the learning algorithm is near-optimal both in physical dynamics accesses and in total evolution time. We construct a single-qubit dephasing Lindbladian family that already requires $Ω(Λ^2/\varepsilon^2)$ channel uses and $Ω(Λ/\varepsilon^2)$ total evolution time, even for adaptive algorithms with arbitrary ancillas and measurements. In particular, the lower bounds imply that the Heisenberg-limited scaling achievable for Hamiltonian learning is information-theoretically impossible once dissipative coefficients must be estimated.

### [135] [Benchmark of quantum algorithms for ground state preparation in the presence of noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20551)
*Daniel Molpeceres,Sirui Lu,J. Ignacio Cirac,Barbara Kraus*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在含噪条件下，利用可精确求解的二次费米子哈密顿量族，系统比较了冷却、绝热和优化算法在基态制备中的性能。研究发现，算法表现依赖于量子相：绝热演化在平凡相中占优，而多频冷却算法在拓扑相（能隙闭合）中具有竞争力或更优。QAOA在平凡相中与冷却相当，但在拓扑相中通常被超越。冷却协议对参数误差具有更强鲁棒性，为含噪量子态制备提供了实用优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在含噪量子设备上高效制备基态是实现量子优势的关键挑战，不同算法在不同噪声条件和系统相图中的表现尚缺乏系统的比较分析。本研究旨在建立一个可扩展的基准测试框架，系统评估冷却、绝热和优化算法在含噪条件下的性能。

Method: 采用可精确求解的二次费米子哈密顿量族，该哈密顿量具有平凡相和拓扑相，中间由量子相变分隔。在退极化噪声模型下，推导了可达相对能量随噪声率变化的标度律，并通过数值模拟验证。系统比较了绝热演化、多频冷却算法和QAOA三种方法的性能。

Result: 绝热演化在平凡相中性能最优；多频冷却算法在拓扑相（能隙闭合区域）中具有竞争力或更优；QAOA在平凡相中与冷却算法性能相当，但在拓扑相中通常被超越。冷却协议对参数不完美性表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 算法性能强烈依赖于系统的量子相特性，不存在普适最优的基态制备算法。冷却协议在拓扑相中的优势及其对参数误差的鲁棒性，使其成为含噪量子态制备的有前景候选方案。本文建立的分析与数值验证框架可推广用于其他基态制备算法的基准测试。

Abstract: We compare the performance of representative cooling, adiabatic, and optimization algorithms for ground-state preparation in the presence of noise. Using an exactly solvable family of quadratic fermionic Hamiltonians subject to depolarizing noise, we derive the scaling of the achievable relative energy as a function of the noise rate and support these results with numerical simulations. The Hamiltonian exhibits two phases, separated by a quantum phase transition. As expected, the performance of the different algorithms depends on the phase: adiabatic evolution is favorable in the trivial phase, while a multi-frequency cooling algorithm, as proposed in [1], becomes competitive or superior in the topological phase, where gap-closing limits adiabatic protocols. We further present numerical results for the quantum approximate optimization algorithm [2], showing that it performs competitively with cooling in the trivial phase but is typically outperformed in the topological regime. Finally, we show that for this model the cooling protocol exhibits enhanced robustness to parameter imperfections, highlighting its potential advantage for realistic implementations of noisy quantum state preparation.
  The analytical approach developed here, in conjunction with numerical validation, establishes an extendable approach to benchmarking ground-state preparation algorithms.

</details>

### [136] [The Kernel of the $\hat A$-Genus in Rational Spin Bordism is Generated by Ricci-Positive Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19505)
*Gerald Höhn,Philipp Höhn*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文证明了在有理Spin配边环中，具有正Ricci曲率流形的配边类恰好张成$\hat A$-genus的核。这一结果回答了复椭圆属背景下关于正Ricci曲率有理配边障碍的问题。证明利用了奇数个二次曲面的光滑完全交簇，并通过$\hat A$-genus的一阶加厚和多项式插值论证得到满秩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答复椭圆属背景下提出的关于正Ricci曲率的有理配边障碍问题：在微分有理Spin范畴中，确定哪些配边类可由正Ricci曲率流形表示。

Method: 使用奇数个$\ell$个二次曲面的光滑完全交$Y_{m,\ell}\subset \mathbb{CP}^{2m+\ell}$（$\ell=1,3,\ldots,2m-1$），这些流形是Spin且Fano的，因而具有正Ricci曲率。通过对$\hat A$-genus进行一阶加厚，在$(J/J^2)_{4m}$上诱导$m-1$个线性泛函，其在$[Y_{m,\ell}]$上的取值由严格递增次数的多项式$P_{m,q}(\ell)$控制，通过多项式插值论证得到满秩。

Result: 在每个度数上，正Ricci曲率Spin流形的配边类的$\mathbb{Q}$-张成恰好等于$\hat A$-genus的核$J$，即$J = \ker(\hat A: R \to \mathbb{Q}[u])$。

Conclusion: 完全解决了有理Spin配边中正Ricci曲率的有理配边障碍刻画问题，证明了$\hat A$-genus是唯一的有理障碍。

Abstract: We prove that, in every degree, the rational Spin bordism classes represented by manifolds admitting metrics with positive Ricci curvature span exactly the kernel of the $\hat A$-genus. More precisely, for \[ R=Ω_*^{Spin}\otimes\mathbb{Q},\qquad J=\ker(\hat A:R\longrightarrow\mathbb{Q}[u]),\] the $\mathbb{Q}$-span of bordism classes of Ricci-positive Spin manifolds equals $J$ in each degree. This answers, in the differentiable rational Spin category, a question about rational bordism obstructions to positive Ricci curvature which was raised in the context of complex elliptic genera.
  The proof uses smooth complete intersections of an odd number $\ell$ of quadrics \[ Y_{m,\ell}\subset \mathbb{CP}^{2m+\ell}, \qquad \ell=1,\, 3,\, \ldots,\, 2m-1. \] These manifolds have real dimension $4m$, are Spin and Fano, and therefore admit metrics with positive Ricci curvature. A first-order thickening of the $\hat A$-genus induces $m-1$ linear functionals on $(J/J^2)_{4m}$. Their values on the classes $[Y_{m,\ell}]$ are governed by polynomials $P_{m,q}(\ell)$ of strictly increasing degrees $q+1=1$, $2$, $\ldots$, $m-1$. This gives full rank by a polynomial-interpolation argument.

</details>

*Tengyang Liu,Yisong Yang*

Method: 对麦克斯韦理论引入尽可能一般的非线性微扰轮廓，使得理论在保持最小偏离麦克斯韦经典形式的同时，能够同时维持三个普适性质（有限能量点电荷、排除磁单极和双荷子、任意小有效半径）。

Result: 该非线性理论满足：点电荷具有有限能量；有限能量的磁单极子和双荷子被排除；点电荷的有效半径可以任意小，从而在局域意义上电荷和能量不可被检测到。

Conclusion: 该非线性电磁理论为电子作为点电荷的不可见性提供了一个经典层面的解释，即其有效半径极小导致局域不可检测性，且该结论不需要量子修正即可成立。

Abstract: We show that a general nonlinearly perturbed Maxwell theory of electromagnetism possesses three universal fundamental properties:
  (i) A finite-energy electric point charge.
  (ii) Exclusion of finite-energy magnetic monopoles and dually charged dyons.
  (iii) Arbitrary smallness of the effective radius of a point electric charge and the associated local undetectedness of the electric charge and energy.
  In particular, this last property offers a classical explanation for the invisibility of the electron, as a point electric charge, in accordance with the smallness of its effective radius.
  This nonlinear theory of electromagnetism has the feature that it minimally perturbs the Maxwell theory with a nonlinearity profile that is as general as possible such that the three universal properties stated above are all maintained.

### [140] [Dirac structures on tangent bundles: a geometric framework for variational principles, constrained dynamics, and symmetry reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20012)
*Hiroaki Yoshimura*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由拉格朗日二形式和约束分布诱导的切丛上的狄拉克结构（拉格朗日-狄拉克结构），为非完整、退化拉格朗日及对称系统提供了统一的几何框架，并发展了相应的变分原理、约化理论及其在带电粒子、电路、理想流体等系统中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在切丛上引入由拉格朗日二形式和约束分布诱导的狄拉克结构；提出切丛上的内蕴变分原理（拉格朗日-达朗贝尔-狄拉克原理）；利用李群对称性发展约化理论，导出约化后的李代数上的狄拉克结构和欧拉-庞加莱-狄拉克方程。

Result: 建立了拉格朗日-狄拉克动力系统的统一几何框架；证明了非完整动力学的规范协变性；推导了约化方程和约化变分原理；通过带电粒子、电路、线性速度拉格朗日系统及理想流体（含不可压约束）验证了理论的有效性。

Conclusion: 拉格朗日-狄拉克结构为包含非完整约束、退化拉格朗日和对称性的复杂力学系统提供了统一的几何和变分描述，并可通过约化和无限维推广应用于更广泛的物理系统。

Abstract: We introduce a Dirac structure on the tangent bundle of a configuration manifold, called a \textit{Lagrange--Dirac structure}, which is naturally induced by the Lagrangian two-form associated with a (possibly degenerate) Lagrangian and a constraint distribution. This structure provides a unified geometric framework for Lagrange--Dirac dynamical systems, encompassing nonholonomic, degenerate Lagrangian, and symmetric systems. In the hyperregular case, the system recovers a first-order formulation of the Lagrange--d'Alembert equations. Although nonholonomic dynamics does not preserve the Lagrangian two-form, we show that the underlying Lagrange--Dirac structure is preserved up to gauge transformations, yielding a natural gauge covariance property.
  We also formulate an intrinsic variational principle directly on the tangent bundle, referred to as the \textit{Lagrange--d'Alembert--Dirac principle}, which recovers Hamilton's principle in the unconstrained case and the Lagrange--d'Alembert principle in the hyperregular constrained case. Furthermore, we develop a reduction theory for systems with Lie group symmetry, deriving a reduced Lagrange--Dirac structure over the Lie algebra that yields the Euler--Poincaré--Dirac equations and a corresponding reduced variational principle. Finally, we illustrate the theory through examples including charged particles, electric circuits, and systems with Lagrangians linear in velocity, and present an infinite-dimensional extension to ideal fluids that naturally incorporates the incompressibility constraint and recovers the Euler equations.

*Jason Bell,Rahim Moosa*

TL;DR: 本文引入"复合基本等平凡"自同构类，证明任何阿贝尔簇的狂野自同构都是此类，反之仅阿贝尔簇的不可约射影簇存在此类狂野自同构，从而证明了Reichstein-Rogalski-Zhang狂野自同构猜想在复合基本等平凡动力系统中的成立，并给出了该猜想到非自治σ-簇情形的反例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受特征零差分域模型论启发，旨在研究代数簇上的自同构类，特别是证明Reichstein、Rogalski和Zhang提出的狂野自同构猜想在复合基本等平凡动力学中的成立。

Method: 通过引入"复合基本等平凡"自同构概念，利用有限序列的等变纤维化从（可能非自治的）代数动力学构造，这些动力学在自身基扩张后平凡化。结合阿贝尔簇的狂野自同构性质进行反向推导。

Result: 证明每个阿贝尔簇的狂野自同构都是复合基本等平凡的；反之，唯一允许复合基本等平凡狂野自同构的不可约射影簇是阿贝尔簇。同时给出该猜想到非自治σ-簇情形的反例。

Conclusion: 在复合基本等平凡动力系统框架下证明了狂野自同构猜想，并指出了该猜想在非自治推广中的局限性。

Abstract: Inspired by the model theory of difference fields in characteristic zero, a class of automorphisms of an algebraic variety, here called compound fundamental isotrivial, is introduced. These are algebraic dynamical systems that are built up via a finite sequence of equivariant fibrations from (possibly nonautonomous) algebraic dynamics which trivialise after base extension over themselves. Every wild automorphism of an abelian variety is compound fundamental isotrivial. Conversely, it is shown that the only irreducible projective varieties admitting a wild automorphism that is compound fundamental isotrivial are the abelian varieties. That is, the wild automorphism conjecture of Reichstein, Rogalski, and Zhang is here proven for compound fundamental isotrivial dynamics. Along the way, a counterexample to the naive generalisation of the conjecture to the nonautonomous setting of $σ$-varieties is provided.

</details>


### [147] [Anti-Zariski pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20268)
*Peng Ren,Eugenii Shustin*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文提出了"反Zariski对"的概念：两条嵌入在射影平面中的代数曲线，虽然它们的补空间同胚，但属于等奇族的不同分支。文章给出了反Zariski对的例子并讨论了相关问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Zariski在1929年发现具有相同度数和奇点集合的曲线可能拓扑不同（即Zariski对）。本文从相反方向出发，提出"反Zariski对"的概念，探究当补空间同胚时曲线是否仍可能属于等奇族的不同分支，从而深化对曲线嵌入拓扑与等奇族结构之间关系的理解。

Method: 本文采用理论分析的方法，定义反Zariski对，通过构造或已知实例展示这种对的存在性，并围绕等奇族、拓扑同胚等概念展开讨论。

Result: 成功给出了反Zariski对的示例，证明了存在这样的曲线对：$(\PP^2,C')$与$(\PP^2,C'')$同胚，但$C'$和$C''$属于等奇族的不同分支。

Conclusion: 反Zariski对的发现补充了经典的Zariski对研究，表明即使曲线在补空间拓扑意义下不可区分，它们在等奇族中仍可能位于不同分支，揭示了奇点与嵌入方式之间更微妙的联系。

Abstract: In 1929, O. Zariski found a pair of complex plane algebraic curves of the same degree and with the same collection of singularities, but embedded into the plane in a topologically different way. Accordingly, such curves belong to different components of the equisingular family. This phenomenon has been intensively studied till now. In this note, we propose a different insight on this subject: Two curves $C',C''\subset\PP^2$ form an {\it anti-Zariski pair}, if $(\PP^2,C')$ and $(\PP^2,C'')$ are homeomorhic, but $C'$ and $C''$ belong to different components of the equisingular family. We exhibit examples of anti-Zariski pairs and discuss related issues.

</details>

### [153] [Lagrangian capacity and chain level string topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20051)
*Shah Faisal,Yin Li*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文推导了具有有限Gutt-Hutchings容量的Liouville域的Lagrangian容量的上界，证明了任意维凸或凹环面的Lagrangian容量等于其对角线，完全解决了Cieliebak-Mohnke关于椭球Lagrangian容量的猜想。证明基于Fukaya-Irie技术的S^1-等变变体，避免了局部切触约束的全纯曲线带来的横截性问题。此外，证明了n维椭球中的极值Lagrangian环面必须位于边界上。应用包括Liouville流形中非球面Lagrangian的宽度新上界以及4维和6维非次临界Weinstein域的Lagrangian容量首次计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Cieliebak-Mohnke关于椭球Lagrangian容量的猜想，并建立一般Liouville域（包括凸/凹环面域）的Lagrangian容量上界理论。

Method: 采用Fukaya-Irie技术的S^1-等变变体，利用Gutt-Hutchings容量推导上界，结合凸/凹环面域的对角线性质，避免使用带局部切触约束的全纯曲线以避免横截性问题。

Result: 完全解决了Cieliebak-Mohnke猜想；凸/凹环面域的Lagrangian容量等于其对角线；n维椭球中极值Lagrangian环面必须位于边界上；给出了Liouville流形中非球面Lagrangian的宽度新上界；首次计算了4维和6维非次临界Weinstein域的Lagrangian容量。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了Lagrangian容量的新上界理论，避免了技术上的横截性困难，并为非次临界Weinstein域的Lagrangian容量计算提供了开创性结果。

Abstract: We derive upper bounds for the Lagrangian capacities of Liouville domains with finite Gutt--Hutchings capacities and show that the Lagrangian capacity of a convex or concave toric domain of arbitrary dimension equals its diagonal. In particular, this completely settles the conjecture of Cieliebak-Mohnke on the Lagrangian capacity of ellipsoids. Our proof is based on an $S^1$-equivariant variant of the techniques of Fukaya and Irie, and does not use holomorphic curves with local tangency constraints, which would inevitably cause transversality issues. Moreover, we show that any extremal Lagrangian torus in an $n$-dimensional ellipsoid must lie on the boundary. Applications of our results and techniques include new upper bounds on the Lagrangian width for aspherical Lagrangians in Liouville manifolds and the first computations of the Lagrangian capacities for many non-subcritical Weinstein domains in dimensions 4 and 6.

### [154] [Fourier-Helgason transform as infinite geodesic time limit in geometric quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20290)
*Ana Cristina Ferreira,Joachim Hilgert,José M. Mourão,João P. Nunes*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文解决了非紧对称空间上Fourier-Helgason变换与几何量子化之间的长期不匹配问题。通过引入量子测地线变换(QGT)，证明了当测地时间趋于无穷时，QGT的极限与FH变换（相差Harish-Chandra c-函数的相位和一个乘法常数）等价，从而统一了Lisiecki在复与非复Lie群情形下的分歧结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lisiecki (1987) 发现对于非复Lie群，水平极化的BKS配对与FH变换不等价且非酉，这与复Lie群情形下的几何解释存在不一致性。本文旨在消除这一分歧，为非复Lie群情形下的FH变换提供正确的几何量子化解释。

Method: (1) 证明水平极化是垂直极化沿测地流前推的无穷时间极限；(2) 将测地流提升为量子丛上的交织酉平行输运，即量子测地线变换(QGT)；(3) 证明QGT在测地时间趋于无穷时存在良定义的极限，且该极限等于FH变换（相差Harish-Chandra c-函数的相位和乘法常数）。

Result: 成功构造了量子测地线变换(QGT)，证明了其无穷时间极限与FH变换等价（模去Harish-Chandra c-函数的相位和乘法常数），为非复Lie群情形下的FH变换提供了统一的几何量子化解释。

Conclusion: 通过引入QGT，解决了非复Lie群情形下几何量子化与FH变换之间的分歧，将Lisiecki的结果推广到了一般非紧对称空间，建立了FH变换与几何量子化之间的精确对应关系。

Abstract: The Fourier-Helgason (FH) transform for a noncompact symmetric space $G/K$ establishes the direct integral decomposition of the unitary representation of $G$ on $L^2(G/K)$ into irreducible principal series representations.
  By applying techniques of geometric quantization to the symplectic manifold $T^*(G/K),$ Lisiecki in 1987 gave a geometric interpretation of the FH transform in the case when $G$ is complex. He defined for general $G$ a ''horizontal'' polarization on $T^*(G/K)$ and showed that, for complex $G$, the Blattner-Kostant-Sternberg (BKS) pairing between the Schrödinger vertical polarization Hilbert space, $L^2(G/K)$, and the Hilbert space of horizontally polarized functions coincides with the FH transform. However, in the same paper, Lisiecki showed that for noncomplex Lie groups the BKS pairing is nonequivalent to the FH transform and nonunitary in general.
  In the present paper, we resolve this discrepancy between the FH transform and geometric quantization in the case when $G$ is not complex.
  First, we show that the horizontal polarization is the infinite-time limit of the push-forward of the vertical polarization with respect to the geodesic flow for a $G$-invariant Riemannian metric. Then we lift the geodesic flow to an intertwining unitary parallel transport on the quantum bundle that we call quantum geodesic transform (QGT). Finally we show that the QGT has a well-defined limit, as the geodesic time goes to infinity, and that it is equal, up to the phase of the Harish-Chandra $c$-function and an irrelevant multiplicative constant, to the FH transform.

</details>

Abstract: We study Gromov's exact-lift two-form method in scalar-curvature geometry. For a closed Riemannian spin manifold carrying a homologically non-trivial closed two-form whose lift to the universal cover is exact, we prove the sharp hyperbolic scalar-curvature comparison with the bottom of the spectrum of the universal Riemannian covering. The two-form enters through Gromov's twisted \(L^2\)-index, which produces harmonic spinors for a family of small unitary twists. We analyze the equality case by interpreting the refined Kato equality defect conformally and use the harmonic spinors to construct a parallel spinor with respect to a suitable conformally related metric. ### [156] [Some constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature metrics on open manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19619)
*Anushree Das*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了开流形上一致正数量曲率完备黎曼度量的若干构造方法。对于n≥3维，若流形存在有界下方的适当Morse函数且无指标≥n-2的临界点，则存在一致正数量曲率度量；若存在正数量曲率度量及极小边界的紧穷竭，则也存在一致正数量曲率度量。对于4≤n≤7维，若流形具有乘积端及C-二次衰减（C>4π²）的正数量曲率度量，则存在足够远的平均凸超曲面可推出一致正数量曲率度量的存在性。应用包括：若不存在一致正数量曲率度量的开流形有正数量曲率度量及平均凸穷竭，则存在紧集的平均凸叶状结构；若具有平均凹穷竭，则端部存在平均凹叶状结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在微分几何中，开流形（非紧完备流形）上一致正数量曲率度量的存在性是一个重要而困难的问题。与紧流形情形相比，开流形上正数量曲率度量的构造受到拓扑与几何边界的多重约束。本文旨在探索在何种拓扑或几何条件下，开流形上已有的正数量曲率度量可以"提升"为一致正数量曲率度量，从而更深入地理解开流形数量曲率的几何刚性。

Method: 本文采用以下方法：(1) Morse理论方法：利用有界下方的适当Morse函数及其临界点指标条件（无指标≥n-2的临界点）来构造一致正数量曲率度量；(2) 几何边界方法：利用极小边界或平均凸/平均凹超曲面的穷竭性质，结合正数量曲率度量的衰减条件（C-二次衰减，C>4π²），通过形变或粘合技术提升曲率下界；(3) 叶状结构方法：通过构造紧集的平均凸/平均凹叶状结构来刻画端部几何性质。

Result: (1) 对于n≥3维开流形，若存在有界下方、无指标≥n-2临界点的适当Morse函数，则存在一致正数量曲率度量。(2) 若存在正数量曲率度量及每个边界为极小的紧穷竭，则也存在一致正数量曲率度量。(3) 对于4≤n≤7维，若流形有乘积端及C-二次衰减（C>4π²）的正数量曲率度量，则存在足够远的平均凸超曲面可推出一致正数量曲率度量。(4) 逆方面：若开流形无一致正数量曲率度量但有正数量曲率度量及平均凸穷竭，则端部存在平均凸叶状结构；若具有平均凹穷竭，则端部存在平均凹叶状结构。

Conclusion: 本文建立了开流形上一致正数量曲率度量存在的若干充分条件，涵盖了Morse理论、极小边界穷竭和平均凸超曲面等多种几何场景。同时给出了不存在一致正数量曲率度量时端部叶状结构的刻画，为正数量曲率开流形的分类与刚性研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: We obtain several constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature complete Riemannian metrics on open manifolds. For dimension $n\geq3$, we show that if such a manifold admits a proper Morse function $f$ bounded below such that $f$ has no critical points of index $\geq n-2$, then it admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. On the other hand if such a manifold admits a positive scalar curvature metric along with a compact exhaustion $\{U_i\}$ such that the boundary of each $U_i$ is minimal, then it also admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. For dimension $4 \leq n\leq 7$, we show that if the manifold has product ends and a positive scalar curvature metric with $C$-quadratic decay at infinity for $C>4π^2$ with respect to some basepoint, then the existence of a mean convex hypersurface far enough from the basepoint implies the existence of a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric on the manifold. We study some applications of these results, including showing that if an open manifold of dimension $n\geq 3$ that admits no uniformly positive scalar curvature metric has a positive scalar curvature metric with mean convex exhaustion, then it admits a mean convex foliation of compact sets sufficiently close to the ends. On the other hand, if such a manifold has a mean concave exhaustion, then its ends admit a mean concave foliation.

</details>

The positive mass theorem plays a key role in finding a solution to the Yamabe equation with minimum energy for the positive curvature case. We mainly focus on the team works in the following three papers [CMY17], [CMY23] and [CC22], on a positive mass theorem in 3-dimensional CR geometry, the CR-Sobolev quotient of Rossi spheres, and the 5-dimensional situation, respectively.

### [160] [Poisson and Jacobi structures from 2-covariant tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20030)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在张量满足适当假设的条件下，推导了关联双向量场的Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的计算公式，将其表达为某分布的曲率项与微分形式的外微分项的组合，从而给出了Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍条件。通过将该框架应用于辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何，恢复了相应的经典括号。最后研究了fat丛和p阶殆余辛结构的情形。

Result: 成功推导了Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的通用计算公式，统一恢复了四种经典几何（辛、局部共形辛、余辛、接触）的括号结构，并刻画了fat丛和p阶殆余辛结构确定Jacobi括号的充要条件。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解Poisson和Jacobi结构提供了统一的几何框架，揭示了不同几何结构中括号的共性本质，并将经典结果作为特例纳入统一理论中。

Abstract: Poisson and Jacobi structures play a fundamental role in the geometric description of many systems arising in classical mechanics. In most cases, the corresponding bivector field is induced by a non-degenerate 2-covariant tensor. In this paper, we present a unified framework for constructing the associated brackets by studying the Poisson and Jacobi structures induced by these tensors. More specifically, under suitable assumptions on the tensor, we derive a formula for computing the Schouten-Nijenhuis bracket of the associated bivector field in terms of the curvature of a certain distribution and the exterior derivative of a differential form. This formula provides the obstruction to the existence of a Poisson or Jacobi structure. To illustrate the theory, we recover the classical brackets associated with symplectic, locally conformally symplectic, cosymplectic, and contact geometries. Finally, we characterize the conditions under which fat bundles and almost cosymplectic structures of order $p$ determine a Jacobi bracket.

However, the uniqueness of the Angenent torus remains a major open problem.
  In this paper, we study rotationally symmetric self-shrinkers of type $\mathbb{S}^{1}\times \mathbb{S}^{n-1}$ from the point of view of ordinary differential equations. We analyze the profile curves of rotationally symmetric self-shrinkers, focusing on the behavior of their vertical points and the curves traced out by these points as the initial height varies. We give a new proof of the existence of the Angenent torus by showing that two families of vertical-point trajectories must intersect.
  We further derive the linearized equation associated with the rotationally symmetric self-shrinker equation and apply a Sturm-type comparison theorem to obtain sufficient conditions for the monotonicity of horizontal-point trajectories. In particular, we prove a comparison theorem for solutions near the spherical self-shrinker $x^{2}+r^{2}=2n$, and establish partial monotonicity results for the curves of horizontal points. ### [163] [The alignment time function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20481)
*Marco van den Beld-Serrano*

TL;DR: 本文研究在稳定因果时空中，给定一个未来指向的类时向量场，是否存在一个时间函数使其梯度与该向量场最优对齐。通过引入一个同时度量向量场与梯度失配程度并惩罚零梯度的泛函，证明了在适当条件下存在唯一光滑的时间函数最小化该泛函，称之为"对齐时间函数"，并建立了其陡度改善、稳定性及对称继承等性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造一个泛函，包含两项：第一项度量类时向量场与Sobolev函数梯度之间的失配程度，第二项用于惩罚零梯度情形。在光滑稳定因果时空的紧致子集上，利用Sobolev空间理论和变分方法，证明该泛函在适当Sobolev指标和惩罚强度条件下存在唯一光滑的极小元。

Conclusion: 对齐时间函数为时空中选择与给定类时向量场最优对齐的时间函数提供了一种规范且稳定的构造方法，具有良好几何性质，在广义相对论的初值问题和时空分层中有潜在应用。

Abstract: Given a fixed past-directed timelike vector field, does there exist a time function whose gradient is optimally aligned with it? We address this question by introducing a functional that, on the one hand, captures the misalignment between the timelike vector field and the gradients of suitable Sobolev functions, and, on the other hand, penalizes null gradients. Our analysis focuses on compact subsets of smooth stably causal spacetimes. More precisely, we prove that, under suitable assumptions on the Sobolev index and the strength of the null gradient penalization, there exists a unique smooth temporal function which minimizes the considered functional. We refer to this minimizer as the \emph{alignment time function}. Furthermore, several useful properties of the alignment time function are established: there exists a canonical procedure to improve its steepness, it is stable under $C^{p}$ convergence of the underlying metrics and vector fields and it inherits the symmetries shared by the metric and the given vector field.

Conclusion: 发展的奇异维度下降方法能有效处理正标量曲率障碍问题，并推广到具有奇异性的AM-PI空间，拓宽了正标量曲率障碍理论的适用范围。

Abstract: In light of recent advances in conformal blow-up methods for the positive mass theorem, including He--Shi--Yu, Bi--Hao--He--Shi--Zhu, and Brendle--Wang, we develop a Schoen--Yau type singular dimension descent method for positive scalar curvature obstructions in arbitrary dimensions. We prove obstructions to positive scalar curvature on enlargeable manifolds and establish the corresponding cubical width inequalities and two-systole estimates. The method also applies to enlargeable AM--PI spaces, giving a positive scalar curvature obstruction when the singular set has Assouad codimension greater than \(3-2/n\).

</details>

*Yumeng Wu,Jie Xiao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用表示簇分层$X(\alpha,m)$上的旗层复形实现PBW基元，通过分析这些层复形限制到子分层时的简单成分，将其与Lusztig构造中出现的单纯反常层$IC(X(\alpha),L_\chi)$进行比较；结合$\mathbb{F}_q$-结构的纯性结果，利用交同上同调复形限制到更小分层时局部系统的重数来刻画转移系数。

Result: 证明了由Lusztig反常层定义的元构成合成代数的一个基；给出了转移矩阵的几何显式描述：从标准基到PBW基的转移矩阵为上三角矩阵，对角元全为1，系数多项式具有正性。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the transition matrix between the PBW basis and the canonical basis for the negative part of the quantized enveloping algebra of the Kronecker quiver from a geometric viewpoint. Our first goal is to give a geometric description of the simple constituents appearing in the restrictions of these flag sheaf complexes to the strata $X(α,m)$. This allows us to compare the PBW-type sheaf complexes with the simple perverse sheaves $IC(X(α),L_χ)$ arising in Lusztig's construction. Using this description together with a purity result for the relevant $\mathbb{F}_q$-structures, we obtain another proof that the elements defined by Lusztig's perverse sheaves indeed form a basis of the composition algebra.Our second goal is to make the transition coefficients between the PBW basis and the canonical basis geometrically explicit. More precisely, we show that these coefficients are governed by the multiplicities of local systems in the restrictions of intersection cohomology complexes to smaller strata. As a consequence, the transition matrix from the canonical basis to the PBW basis is upper triangular with diagonal entries equal to $1$, and its coefficients admit a direct geometric interpretation. In particular, in the Kronecker quiver case we recover the triangularity of the transition matrix and obtain positivity properties of the corresponding coefficient polynomials.

Abstract: We prove several results about Stiefel-Whitney Classes (SWCs) $w_k(π)$ of representations $π$ of $S_n$. First, each SWC is polynomial in the character values of $π$ at involutions. Abstract: Let $\mathfrak{g}=\mathfrak{g}(A)$ be the Borcherds-Kac-Moody Lie algebra (BKM LA), corresponding to a BKM Cartan matrix $A$ filled by negative integers. Let $P^+\subset \mathfrak{h}^*$ the classical dominant integral cone (wherein pairings are non-negative). The non-integrable simple highest weight modules $L(μ)$'s widely studied were broadly those by Naito ([Trans. Amer. Soc., 1995]), for $μ$'s dot-linked to $P^+$-translates of sums $- \sum_{j\in J}α_j$ of mutually orthogonal and imaginary simple roots $α_j$'s.

These needed a family of ``integrable'' $L(μ)$'s for $μ$'s inside our novel signed-dominant-integral cone $P^{\pm}$ (which generalizes $P^+$). Pairings $μ(α_i^{\vee})\leq 0$ therein are multiples of $\frac{A_{ii}}{2}$ for all $i$. Nevertheless, $L(μ)$ contain ``Chevalley-Serre relations'' $f_i^{\frac{2}{A_{ii}}{μ(α_i^{\vee})}+1}L(μ)_μ=0$; which differ from relations in $L(λ)$ for all $λ\in P^+$, and are seemingly unstudied earlier (also by Naito).
  This paper initiates the study in rank-2, of the module structures and maximal vectors (or Verma embeddings) in the Verma covers $M(μ)$ of $L(μ)$'s for $μ\in P^{\pm}$. In this, our goal is to explore in weight spaces of those Verma covers, the strictness (or otherwise, an uniform equality) of lower bounds by Kac and Kazhdan ([Adv. Math., 1979]) for count of linearly independent maximal vectors. We obtain presentations and characters of all $V$'s when Kac-Kazhdan equation has unique solution in the interior of root-cone. This builds on the unique solution case in Lemma 3.1 from that paper.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: t-结构（特别是由silting/tilting对象诱导的）在三角范畴研究中具有核心地位，且与导出等价紧密相关。本文旨在Q-形导出范畴中构造具有良好性质的t-结构，并研究其与silting对象及组合条件的关系。

Method: 利用Saorín-Šťovíček建立的Frobenius正合范畴中余遗传余挠对与其稳定范畴中t-结构之间的对应关系，在Q-形导出范畴中通过Q的可容许划分构造t-结构；描述双纤维对象构成的Frobenius正合范畴中对应的余挠对，并由同调消没条件识别余层；通过silting对象刻画这些t-结构。

Result: 成功构造了一族由Q的可容许划分诱导的t-结构，给出了相应余挠对和余层的显式描述；证明了这些t-结构由silting对象诱导，该silting对象可由Q的组合结构完全确定；在循环箭图等情形下验证了组合条件失效时范畴可能不含非平凡t-结构，与Linckelmann在稳定模范畴中的现象类似。

Conclusion: 本文建立的t-结构框架可恢复Q-形导出范畴中已知的等价关系，同时揭示了该范畴中t-结构的存在性与Q的组合结构（如无环条件）之间的本质联系，丰富了三角范畴中t-结构理论的研究。

Abstract: Torsion pairs, and in particular t-structures, play a central role in the study of triangulated categories. Specifically, t-structures induced by silting (or tilting) objects often admit desirable properties with strong connections to derived equivalences. In this paper, using the correspondence of Saorín-Šťovíček between cohereditary cotorsion pairs in Frobenius exact categories and t-structures in their stable categories, we construct a family of t-structures in the $Q$-shaped derived category of Holm and Jorgensen, arising from admissible partitions of $Q$. We give an explicit description of the associated cotorsion pairs inside the Frobenius exact category of the bifibrant objects, and we identify the corresponding co-aisles by certain homological vanishing conditions. Such t-structures are proved to be induced by a silting object, that can be completely determined by the combinatorics of $Q$. Finally, we illustrate our results by recovering well-known equivalences in the $Q$-shaped setting, while also providing examples where the combinatorial conditions fail (e.g. cyclic quivers), showing that such categories may admit no non-trivial t-structures, revealing phenomena analogous to those observed by Linckelmann in stable module categories.

</details>
